viśalyau tu mahātmānau tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇauc asaṃbhrāntau jagṛhatus tāv ubhau dhanuṣī varea tato visphārayāṇasya rāmasya dhanur uttamamc babhūva tumulaḥ śabdo rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvahaḥa aśobhata tadā rāmo dhanur visphārayan mahatc bhagavān iva saṃkruddho bhavo vedamayaṃ dhanuḥa vānarodghuṣṭaghoṣaś ca rākṣasānāṃ ca nisvanaḥc jyāśabdaś cāpi rāmasya trayaṃ vyāpa diśo daśaa tasya kārmukamuktaiś ca śarais tatpuragopuramc kailāsaśṛṅgapratimaṃ vikīrṇam apatad bhuvia tato rāmaśarān dṛṣṭvā vimāneṣu gṛheṣu cac saṃnāho rākṣasendrāṇāṃ tumulaḥ samapadyataa teṣāṃ saṃnahyamānānāṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca kurvatāmc śarvarī rākṣasendrāṇāṃ raudrīva samapadyataa ādiṣṭā vānarendrās te sugrīveṇa mahātmanāc āsannā dvāram āsādya yudhyadhvaṃ plavagarṣabhāḥa yaś ca vo vitathaṃ kuryāt tatra tatra vyavasthitaḥc sa hantavyo bhisaṃplutya rājaśāsanadūṣakaḥa teṣu vānaramukhyeṣu dīptolkojjvalapāṇiṣuc sthiteṣu dvāram āsādya rāvaṇaṃ manyur āviśata tasya jṛmbhitavikṣepād vyāmiśrā vai diśo daśac rūpavān iva rudrasya manyur gātreṣv adṛśyataa sa nikumbhaṃ ca kumbhaṃ ca kumbhakarṇātmajāv ubhauc preṣayām āsa saṃkruddho rākṣasair bahubhiḥ sahaa śaśāsa caiva tān sarvān rākṣasān rākṣaseśvaraḥc rākṣasā gacchatātraiva siṃhanādaṃ ca nādayana tatas tu coditās tena rākṣasā jvalitāyudhāḥc laṅkāyā niryayur vīrāḥ praṇadantaḥ punaḥ punaḥa bhīmāśvarathamātaṃgaṃ nānāpatti samākulamc dīptaśūlagadākhaḍgaprāsatomarakārmukama tad rākṣasabalaṃ ghoraṃ bhīmavikramapauruṣamc dadṛśe jvalitaprāsaṃ kiṅkiṇīśatanāditama hemajālācitabhujaṃ vyāveṣṭitaparaśvadhamc vyāghūrṇitamahāśastraṃ bāṇasaṃsaktakārmukama gandhamālyamadhūtsekasaṃmodita mahānilamc ghoraṃ śūrajanākīrṇaṃ mahāmbudharanisvanama taṃ dṛṣṭvā balam āyāntaṃ rākṣasānāṃ sudāruṇamc saṃcacāla plavaṃgānāṃ balam uccair nanāda caa javenāplutya ca punas tad rākṣasabalaṃ mahatc abhyayāt pratyaribalaṃ pataṃga iva pāvakama teṣāṃ bhujaparāmarśavyāmṛṣṭaparighāśanic rākṣasānāṃ balaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhūyastaram aśobhataa tathaivāpy apare teṣāṃ kapīnām asibhiḥ śitaiḥc pravīrān abhito jaghnur ghorarūpā niśācarāḥa ghnantam anyaṃ jaghānānyaḥ pātayantam apātayatc garhamāṇaṃ jagarhānye daśantam apare daśata dehīty anye dadāty anyo dadāmīty aparaḥ punaḥc kiṃ kleśayasi tiṣṭheti tatrānyonyaṃ babhāṣirea samudyatamahāprāsaṃ muṣṭiśūlāsisaṃkulamc prāvartata mahāraudraṃ yuddhaṃ vānararakṣasāma vānarān daśa sapteti rākṣasā abhyapātayanc rākṣasān daśasapteti vānarā jaghnur āhavea visrastakeśarasanaṃ vimuktakavacadhvajamc balaṃ rākṣasam ālambya vānarāḥ paryavārayana pravṛtte saṃkule tasmin ghore vīrajanakṣayec aṅgadaḥ kampanaṃ vīram āsasāda raṇotsukaḥa āhūya so ṅgadaṃ kopāt tāḍayām āsa vegitaḥc gadayā kampanaḥ pūrvaṃ sa cacāla bhṛśāhataḥa sa saṃjñāṃ prāpya tejasvī cikṣepa śikharaṃ gireḥc arditaś ca prahāreṇa kampanaḥ patito bhuvia hatapravīrā vyathitā rākṣasendracamūs tadāc jagāmābhimukhī sā tu kumbhakarṇasuto yataḥe āpatantīṃ ca vegena kumbhas tāṃ sāntvayac camūma sa dhanur dhanvināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya susamāhitaḥc mumocāśīviṣaprakhyāñ śarān dehavidāraṇāna tasya tac chuśubhe bhūyaḥ saśaraṃ dhanur uttamamc vidyudairāvatārciṣmad dvitīyendradhanur yathāa ākarṇakṛṣṭamuktena jaghāna dvividaṃ tadāc tena hāṭakapuṅkhena patriṇā patravāsasāa sahasābhihatas tena vipramuktapadaḥ sphuranc nipapātādrikūṭābho vihvalaḥ plavagottamaḥa maindas tu bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagnaṃ tatra mahāhavec abhidudrāva vegena pragṛhya mahatīṃ śilāma tāṃ śilāṃ tu pracikṣepa rākṣasāya mahābalaḥc bibheda tāṃ śilāṃ kumbhaḥ prasannaiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥa saṃdhāya cānyaṃ sumukhaṃ śaram āśīviṣopamamc ājaghāna mahātejā vakṣasi dvividāgrajama sa tu tena prahāreṇa maindo vānarayūthapaḥc marmaṇy abhihatas tena papāta bhuvi mūrchitaḥa aṅgado mātulau dṛṣṭvā patitau tau mahābalauc abhidudrāva vegena kumbham udyatakārmukama tam āpatantaṃ vivyādha kumbhaḥ pañcabhir āyasaiḥc tribhiś cānyaiḥ śitair bāṇair mātaṃgam iva tomaraiḥa so ṅgadaṃ vividhair bāṇaiḥ kumbho vivyādha vīryavānc akuṇṭhadhārair niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ kanakabhūṣaṇaiḥa aṅgadaḥ pratividdhāṅgo vāliputro na kampatec śilāpādapavarṣāṇi tasya mūrdhni vavarṣa haa sa praciccheda tān sarvān bibheda ca punaḥ śilāḥc kumbhakarṇātmajaḥ śrīmān vāliputrasamīritāna āpatantaṃ ca saṃprekṣya kumbho vānarayūthapamc bhruvor vivyādha bāṇābhyām ulkābhyām iva kuñjarama aṅgadaḥ pāṇinā netre pidhāya rudhirokṣitec sālam āsannam ekena parijagrāha pāṇināa tam indraketupratimaṃ vṛkṣaṃ mandarasaṃnibhamc samutsṛjantaṃ vegena paśyatāṃ sarvarakṣasāma sa ciccheda śitair bāṇaiḥ saptabhiḥ kāyabhedanaiḥc aṅgado vivyathe bhīkṣṇaṃ sasāda ca mumoha caa aṅgadaṃ vyathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sīdantam iva sāgarec durāsadaṃ hariśreṣṭhā rāghavāya nyavedayana rāmas tu vyathitaṃ śrutvā vāliputraṃ mahāhavec vyādideśa hariśreṣṭhāñ jāmbavatpramukhāṃs tataḥa te tu vānaraśārdūlāḥ śrutvā rāmasya śāsanamc abhipetuḥ susaṃkruddhāḥ kumbham udyatakārmukama tato drumaśilāhastāḥ kopasaṃraktalocanāḥc rirakṣiṣanto bhyapatann aṅgadaṃ vānararṣabhāḥa jāmbavāṃś ca suṣeṇaś ca vegadarśī ca vānaraḥc kumbhakarṇātmajaṃ vīraṃ kruddhāḥ samabhidudruvuḥa samīkṣyātatatas tāṃs tu vānarendrān mahābalānc āvavāra śaraugheṇa nageneva jalāśayama tasya bāṇacayaṃ prāpya na śoker ativartitumc vānarendrā mahātmāno velām iva mahodadhiḥa tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā harigaṇāñ śaravṛṣṭibhir arditānc aṅgadaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā bhrātṛjaṃ plavageśvaraḥa abhidudrāva vegena sugrīvaḥ kumbham āhavec śailasānu caraṃ nāgaṃ vegavān iva kesarīa utpāṭya ca mahāśailān aśvakarṇān dhavān bahūnc anyāṃś ca vividhān vṛkṣāṃś cikṣepa ca mahābalaḥa tāṃ chādayantīm ākāśaṃ vṛkṣavṛṣṭiṃ durāsadāmc kumbhakarṇātmajaḥ śrīmāṃś ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa abhilakṣyeṇa tīvreṇa kumbhena niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc ācitās te drumā rejur yathā ghorāḥ śataghnayaḥa drumavarṣaṃ tu tac chinnaṃ dṛṣṭvā kumbhena vīryavānc vānarādhipatiḥ śrīmān mahāsattvo na vivyathea nirbhidyamānaḥ sahasā sahamānaś ca tāñ śarānc kumbhasya dhanur ākṣipya babhañjendradhanuḥprabhama avaplutya tataḥ śīghraṃ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaramc abravīt kupitaḥ kumbhaṃ bhagnaśṛṅgam iva dvipama nikumbhāgraja vīryaṃ te bāṇavegaṃ tad adbhutamc saṃnatiś ca prabhāvaś ca tava vā rāvaṇasya vāa prahrādabalivṛtraghnakuberavaruṇopamac ekas tvam anujāto si pitaraṃ balavattaraḥa tvām evaikaṃ mahābāhuṃ śūlahastam ariṃdamamc tridaśā nātivartante jitendriyam ivādhayaḥa varadānāt pitṛvyas te sahate devadānavānc kumbhakarṇas tu vīryeṇa sahate ca surāsurāna dhanuṣīndrajitas tulyaḥ pratāpe rāvaṇasya cac tvam adya rakṣasāṃ loke śreṣṭho si balavīryataḥa mahāvimardaṃ samare mayā saha tavādbhutamc adya bhūtāni paśyantu śakraśambarayor ivaa kṛtam apratimaṃ karma darśitaṃ cāstrakauśalamc pātitā harivīrāś ca tvayaite bhīmavikramāḥa upālambhabhayāc cāpi nāsi vīra mayā hataḥc kṛtakarmā pariśrānto viśrāntaḥ paśya me balama tena sugrīvavākyena sāvamānena mānitaḥc agner ājyahutasyeva tejas tasyābhyavardhataa tataḥ kumbhaḥ samutpatya sugrīvam abhipadya cac ājaghānorasi kruddho vajravegena muṣṭināa tasya carma ca pusphoṭa saṃjajñe cāsya śoṇitamc sa ca muṣṭir mahāvegaḥ pratijaghne sthimaṇḍalea tadā vegena tatrāsīt tejaḥ prajvālitaṃ muhuḥc vajraniṣpeṣasaṃjātajvālā merau yathā giraua sa tatrābhihatas tena sugrīvo vānararṣabhaḥc muṣṭiṃ saṃvartayām āsa vajrakalpaṃ mahābalaḥa arciḥsahasravikacaṃ ravimaṇḍalasaprabhamc sa muṣṭiṃ pātayām āsa kumbhasyorasi vīryavāna muṣṭinābhihatas tena nipapātāśu rākṣasaḥc lohitāṅga ivākāśād dīptaraśmir yadṛcchayāa kumbhasya patato rūpaṃ bhagnasyorasi muṣṭināc babhau rudrābhipannasya yathārūpaṃ gavāṃ pateḥa tasmin hate bhīmaparākrameṇaplavaṃgamānām ṛṣabheṇa yuddhec mahī saśailā savanā cacālabhayaṃ ca rakṣāṃsy adhikaṃ viveśaa nikumbho bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīveṇa nipātitamc pradahann iva kopena vānarendram avaikṣataa tataḥ sragdāmasaṃnaddhaṃ dattapañcāṅgulaṃ śubhamc ādade parighaṃ vīro nagendraśikharopamama hemapaṭṭaparikṣiptaṃ vajravidrumabhūṣitamc yamadaṇḍopamaṃ bhīmaṃ rakṣasāṃ bhayanāśanama tam āvidhya mahātejāḥ śakradhvajasamaṃ raṇec vinanāda vivṛttāsyo nikumbho bhīmavikramaḥa urogatena niṣkeṇa bhujasthair aṅgadair apic kuṇḍalābhyāṃ ca mṛṣṭābhyāṃ mālayā ca vicitrayāa nikumbho bhūṣaṇair bhāti tena sma parigheṇa cac yathendradhanuṣā meghaḥ savidyutstanayitnumāna parighāgreṇa pusphoṭa vātagranthir mahātmanaḥc prajajvāla saghoṣaś ca vidhūma iva pāvakaḥa nagaryā viṭapāvatyā gandharvabhavanottamaiḥc saha caivāmarāvatyā sarvaiś ca bhavanaiḥ sahaa satārāgaṇanakṣatraṃ sacandraṃ samahāgrahamc nikumbhaparighāghūrṇaṃ bhramatīva nabhastalama durāsadaś ca saṃjajñe parighābharaṇaprabhaḥc krodhendhano nikumbhāgnir yugāntāgnir ivotthitaḥa rākṣasā vānarāś cāpi na śekuḥ spandituṃ bhayātc hanūmaṃs tu vivṛtyoras tasthau pramukhato balīa parighopamabāhus tu parighaṃ bhāskaraprabhamc balī balavatas tasya pātayām āsa vakṣasia sthire tasyorasi vyūḍhe parighaḥ śatadhā kṛtaḥc viśīryamāṇaḥ sahasā ulkā śatam ivāmbarea sa tu tena prahāreṇa cacāla ca mahākapiḥc parigheṇa samādhūto yathā bhūmicale calaḥa sa tathābhihatas tena hanūmān plavagottamaḥc muṣṭiṃ saṃvartayām āsa balenātimahābalaḥa tam udyamya mahātejā nikumbhorasi vīryavānc abhicikṣepa vegena vegavān vāyuvikramaḥa tataḥ pusphoṭa carmāsya prasusrāva ca śoṇitamc muṣṭinā tena saṃjajñe jvālā vidyud ivotthitāa sa tu tena prahāreṇa nikumbho vicacāla hac svasthaś cāpi nijagrāha hanūmantaṃ mahābalama vicukruśus tadā saṃkhye bhīmaṃ laṅkānivāsinaḥc nikumbhenoddhṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmantaṃ mahābalama sa tathā hriyamāṇo pi kumbhakarṇātmajena hic ājaghānānilasuto vajravegena muṣṭināa ātmānaṃ mocayitvātha kṣitāv abhyavapadyatac hanūmān unmamathāśu nikumbhaṃ mārutātmajaḥa nikṣipya paramāyatto nikumbhaṃ niṣpipeṣa cac utpatya cāsya vegena papātorasi vīryavāna parigṛhya ca bāhubhyāṃ parivṛtya śirodharāmc utpāṭayām āsa śiro bhairavaṃ nadato mahata atha vinadati sādite nikumbhepavanasutena raṇe babhūva yuddhamc daśarathasutarākṣasendracamvorbhṛśataram āgataroṣayoḥ subhīmama nikumbhaṃ ca hataṃ śrutvā kumbhaṃ ca vinipātitamc rāvaṇaḥ paramāmarṣī prajajvālānalo yathāa nairṛtaḥ krodhaśokābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ tu parimūrchitaḥc kharaputraṃ viśālākṣaṃ makarākṣam acodayata gaccha putra mayājñapto balenābhisamanvitaḥc rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva jahi tau savanaukasaua rāvaṇasya vacaḥ śrutvā śūro mānī kharātmajaḥc bāḍham ity abravīd dhṛṣṭo makarākṣo niśācaraḥa so bhivādya daśagrīvaṃ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇamc nirjagāma gṛhāc chubhrād rāvaṇasyājñayā balīa samīpasthaṃ balādhyakṣaṃ kharaputro bravīd idamc ratham ānīyatāṃ śīghraṃ sainyaṃ cānīyatāṃ tvarāta tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā balādhyakṣo niśācaraḥc syandanaṃ ca balaṃ caiva samīpaṃ pratyapādayata pradakṣiṇaṃ rathaṃ kṛtvā āruroha niśācaraḥc sūtaṃ saṃcodayām āsa śīghraṃ me ratham āvahaa atha tān rākṣasān sarvān makarākṣo bravīd idamc yūyaṃ sarve prayudhyadhvaṃ purastān mama rākṣasāḥa ahaṃ rākṣasarājena rāvaṇena mahātmanāc ājñaptaḥ samare hantuṃ tāv ubhau rāmalakṣmaṇaua adya rāmaṃ vadhiṣyāmi lakṣmaṇaṃ ca niśācarāḥc śākhāmṛgaṃ ca sugrīvaṃ vānarāṃś ca śarottamaiḥa adya śūlanipātaiś ca vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūmc pradahiṣyāmi saṃprāptāṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥa makarākṣasya tac chrutvā vacanaṃ te niśācarāḥc sarve nānāyudhopetā balavantaḥ samāhitāḥa te kāmarūpiṇaḥ śūrā daṃṣṭriṇaḥ piṅgalekṣaṇāḥc mātaṃgā iva nardanto dhvastakeśā bhayānakāḥa parivārya mahākāyā mahākāyaṃ kharātmajamc abhijagmus tadā hṛṣṭāś cālayanto vasuṃdharāma śaṅkhabherīsahasrāṇām āhatānāṃ samantataḥc kṣveḍitāsphoṭitānāṃ ca tataḥ śabdo mahān abhūta prabhraṣṭo tha karāt tasya pratodaḥ sārathes tadāc papāta sahasā caiva dhvajas tasya ca rakṣasaḥa tasya te rathasaṃyuktā hayā vikramavarjitāḥc caraṇair ākulair gatvā dīnāḥ sāsramukhā yayuḥa pravāti pavanas tasya sapāṃsuḥ kharadāruṇaḥc niryāṇe tasya raudrasya makarākṣasya durmateḥa tāni dṛṣṭvā nimittāni rākṣasā vīryavattamāḥc acintyanirgatāḥ sarve yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇaua ghanagajamahiṣāṅgatulyavarṇāḥsamaramukheṣv asakṛd gadāsibhinnāḥc aham aham iti yuddhakauśalās terajanicarāḥ paribabhramur nadantaḥa nirgataṃ makarākṣaṃ te dṛṣṭvā vānarapuṃgavāḥc āplutya sahasā sarve yoddhukāmā vyavasthitāḥa tataḥ pravṛttaṃ sumahat tad yuddhaṃ lomaharṣaṇamc niśācaraiḥ plavaṃgānāṃ devānāṃ dānavair ivaa vṛkṣaśūlanipātaiś ca śilāparighapātanaiḥc anyonyaṃ mardayanti sma tadā kapiniśācarāḥa śaktiśūlagadākhaḍgais tomaraiś ca niśācarāḥc paṭṭasair bhindipālaiś ca bāṇapātaiḥ samantataḥa pāśamudgaradaṇḍaiś ca nirghātaiś cāparais tathāc kadanaṃ kapisiṃhānāṃ cakrus te rajanīcarāḥa bāṇaughair arditāś cāpi kharaputreṇa vānarāḥc saṃbhrāntamanasaḥ sarve dudruvur bhayapīḍitāḥa tān dṛṣṭvā rākṣasāḥ sarve dravamāṇān vanaukasaḥc nedus te siṃhavad dhṛṣṭā rākṣasā jitakāśinaḥa vidravatsu tadā teṣu vānareṣu samantataḥc rāmas tān vārayām āsa śaravarṣeṇa rākṣasāna vāritān rākṣasān dṛṣṭvā makarākṣo niśācaraḥc krodhān alasam āviṣṭo vacanaṃ cedam abravīta tiṣṭha rāma mayā sārdhaṃ dvandvayuddhaṃ dadāmi tec tyājayiṣyāmi te prāṇān dhanurmuktaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥa yat tadā daṇḍakāraṇye pitaraṃ hatavān mamac madagrataḥ svakarmasthaṃ smṛtvā roṣo bhivardhatea dahyante bhṛśam aṅgāni durātman mama rāghavac yan mayāsi na dṛṣṭas tvaṃ tasmin kāle mahāvanea diṣṭyāsi darśanaṃ rāma mama tvaṃ prāptavān ihac kāṅkṣito si kṣudhārtasya siṃhasyevetaro mṛgaḥa adya madbāṇavegena pretarāḍ viṣayaṃ gataḥc ye tvayā nihatāḥ śūrāḥ saha tais tvaṃ sameṣyasia bahunātra kim uktena śṛṇu rāma vaco mamac paśyantu sakalā lokās tvāṃ māṃ caiva raṇājirea astrair vā gadayā vāpi bāhubhyāṃ vā mahāhavec abhyastaṃ yena vā rāma tena vā vartatāṃ yudhia makarākṣavacaḥ śrutvā rāmo daśarathātmajaḥc abravīt prahasan vākyam uttarottaravādinama caturdaśasahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ tvatpitā ca yaḥc triśirā dūṣaṇaś cāpi daṇḍake nihatā mayāa svāśitās tava māṃsena gṛdhragomāyuvāyasāḥc bhaviṣyanty adya vai pāpa tīkṣṇatuṇḍanakhāṅkuśāḥa evam uktas tu rāmeṇa kharaputro niśācaraḥc bāṇaughān asṛjat tasmai rāghavāya raṇājirea tāñ śarāñ śaravarṣeṇa rāmaś ciccheda naikadhāc nipetur bhuvi te chinnā rukmapuṅkhāḥ sahasraśaḥa tad yuddham abhavat tatra sametyānyonyam ojasāc khara rākṣasaputrasya sūnor daśarathasya caa jīmūtayor ivākāśe śabdo jyātalayos tadāc dhanur muktaḥ svanotkṛṣṭaḥ śrūyate ca raṇājirea devadānavagandharvāḥ kiṃnarāś ca mahoragāḥc antarikṣagatāḥ sarve draṣṭukāmās tad adbhutama viddham anyonyagātreṣu dviguṇaṃ vardhate balamc kṛtapratikṛtānyonyaṃ kurvāte tau raṇājirea rāmam uktās tu bāṇaughān rākṣasas tv acchinad raṇec rakṣomuktāṃs tu rāmo vai naikadhā prācchinac charaiḥa bāṇaughavitatāḥ sarvā diśaś ca vidiśas tathāc saṃchannā vasudhā caiva samantān na prakāśatea tataḥ kruddho mahābāhur dhanuś ciccheda rakṣasaḥc aṣṭābhir atha nārācaiḥ sūtaṃ vivyādha rāghavaḥe bhittvā śarai rathaṃ rāmo rathāśvān samapātayata viratho vasudhāṃ tiṣṭhan makarākṣo niśācaraḥc atiṣṭhad vasudhāṃ rakṣaḥ śūlaṃ jagrāha pāṇināe trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhama vibhrāmya ca mahac chūlaṃ prajvalantaṃ niśācaraḥc sa krodhāt prāhiṇot tasmai rāghavāya mahāhavea tam āpatantaṃ jvalitaṃ kharaputrakarāc cyutamc bāṇais tu tribhir ākāśe śūlaṃ ciccheda rāghavaḥa sacchinno naikadhā śūlo divyahāṭakamaṇḍitaḥc vyaśīryata mahokleva rāmabāṇārdito bhuvia tac chūlaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇādbhutakarmaṇāc sādhu sādhv iti bhūtāni vyāharanti nabhogatāḥa tad dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ śūlaṃ makarākṣo niśācaraḥc muṣṭim udyamya kākutsthaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīta sa taṃ dṛṣṭvā patantaṃ vai prahasya raghunandanaḥc pāvakāstraṃ tato rāmaḥ saṃdadhe svaśarāsanea tenāstreṇa hataṃ rakṣaḥ kākutsthena tadā raṇec saṃchinnahṛdayaṃ tatra papāta ca mamāra caa dṛṣṭvā te rākṣasāḥ sarve makarākṣasya pātanamc laṅkām eva pradhāvanta rāmabālārditās tadāa daśarathanṛpaputrabāṇavegairajanicaraṃ nihataṃ kharātmajaṃ tamc dadṛśur atha ca devatāḥ prahṛṣṭāgirim iva vajrahataṃ yathā viśīrṇama makarākṣaṃ hataṃ śrutvā rāvaṇaḥ samitiṃjayaḥc ādideśātha saṃkruddho raṇāyendrajitaṃ sutama jahi vīra mahāvīryau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇauc adṛśyo dṛśyamāno vā sarvathā tvaṃ balādhikaḥa tvam apratimakarmāṇam indraṃ jayasi saṃyugec kiṃ punar mānuṣau dṛṣṭvā na vadhiṣyasi saṃyugea tathokto rākṣasendreṇa pratigṛhya pitur vacaḥc yajñabhūmau sa vidhivat pāvakaṃ juhuve ndrajita juhvataś cāpi tatrāgniṃ raktoṣṇīṣadharāḥ striyaḥc ājagmus tatra saṃbhrāntā rākṣasyo yatra rāvaṇiḥa śastrāṇi śarapatrāṇi samidho tha vibhītakāḥc lohitāni ca vāsāṃsi sruvaṃ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tathāa sarvato gniṃ samāstīrya śarapatraiḥ samantataḥc chāgasya sarvakṛṣṇasya galaṃ jagrāha jīvataḥa caruhomasamiddhasya vidhūmasya mahārciṣaḥc babhūvus tāni liṅgāni vijayaṃ darśayanti caa pradakṣiṇāvartaśikhas taptahāṭakasaṃnibhaḥc havis tat pratijagrāha pāvakaḥ svayam utthitaḥa hutvāgniṃ tarpayitvātha devadānavarākṣasānc āruroha rathaśreṣṭham antardhānagataṃ śubhama sa vājibhiś caturbhis tu bāṇaiś ca niśitair yutaḥc āropitamahācāpaḥ śuśubhe syandanottamea jājvalyamāno vapuṣā tapanīyaparicchadaḥc śaraiś candrārdhacandraiś ca sa rathaḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥa jāmbūnadamahākambur dīptapāvakasaṃnibhaḥc babhūvendrajitaḥ ketur vaidūryasamalaṃkṛtaḥa tena cādityakalpena brahmāstreṇa ca pālitaḥc sa babhūva durādharṣo rāvaṇiḥ sumahābalaḥa so bhiniryāya nagarād indrajit samitiṃjayaḥc hutvāgniṃ rākṣasair mantrair antardhānagato bravīta adya hatvāhave yau tau mithyā pravrajitau vanec jayaṃ pitre pradāsyāmi rāvaṇāya raṇādhikama kṛtvā nirvānarām urvīṃ hatvā rāmaṃ salakṣmaṇamc kariṣye paramāṃ prītim ity uktvāntaradhīyataa āpapātātha saṃkruddho daśagrīveṇa coditaḥc tīkṣṇakārmukanārācais tīkṣṇas tv indraripū raṇea sa dadarśa mahāvīryau nāgau triśirasāv ivac sṛjantāv iṣujālāni vīrau vānaramadhyagaua imau tāv iti saṃcintya sajyaṃ kṛtvā ca kārmukamc saṃtatāneṣudhārābhiḥ parjanya iva vṛṣṭimāna sa tu vaihāyasaṃ prāpya saratho rāmalakṣmaṇauc acakṣur viṣaye tiṣṭhan vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tau tasya śaravegena parītau rāmalakṣmaṇauc dhanuṣī saśare kṛtvā divyam astraṃ pracakratuḥa pracchādayantau gaganaṃ śarajālair mahābalauc tam astraiḥ surasaṃkāśau naiva pasparśatuḥ śaraiḥa sa hi dhūmāndhakāraṃ ca cakre pracchādayan nabhaḥc diśaś cāntardadhe śrīmān nīhāratamasāvṛtaḥa naiva jyātalanirghoṣo na ca nemikhurasvanaḥc śuśruve caratas tasya na ca rūpaṃ prakāśatea ghanāndhakāre timire śaravarṣam ivādbhutamc sa vavarṣa mahābāhur nārācaśaravṛṣṭibhiḥa sa rāmaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaiḥ śarair dattavaro bhṛśamc vivyādha samare kruddhaḥ sarvagātreṣu rāvaṇiḥa tau hanyamānau nārācair dhārābhir iva parvatauc hemapuṅkhān naravyāghrau tigmān mumucatuḥ śarāna antarikṣaṃ samāsādya rāvaṇiṃ kaṅkapatriṇaḥc nikṛtya patagā bhūmau petus te śoṇitokṣitāḥa atimātraṃ śaraugheṇa pīḍyamānau narottamauc tān iṣūn patato bhallair anekair nicakartatuḥa yato hi dadṛśāte tau śarān nipatitāñ śitānc tatas tato dāśarathī sasṛjāte stram uttamama rāvaṇis tu diśaḥ sarvā rathenātirathaḥ patanc vivyādha tau dāśarathī laghv astro niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa tenātividdhau tau vīrau rukmapuṅkhaiḥ susaṃhataiḥc babhūvatur dāśarathī puṣpitāv iva kiṃśukaua nāsya veda gatiṃ kaś cin na ca rūpaṃ dhanuḥ śarānc na cānyad viditaṃ kiṃ cit sūryasyevābhrasaṃplavea tena viddhāś ca harayo nihatāś ca gatāsavaḥc babhūvuḥ śataśas tatra patitā dharaṇītalea lakṣmaṇas tu susaṃkruddho bhrātaraṃ vākyam abravītc brāhmam astraṃ prayokṣyāmi vadhārthaṃ sarvarakṣasāma tam uvāca tato rāmo lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇamc naikasya heto rakṣāṃsi pṛthivyāṃ hantum arhasia ayudhyamānaṃ pracchannaṃ prāñjaliṃ śaraṇāgatamc palāyantaṃ pramattaṃ vā na tvaṃ hantum ihārhasia asyaiva tu vadhe yatnaṃ kariṣyāvo mahābalac ādekṣyāvo mahāvegān astrān āśīviṣopamāna tam enaṃ māyinaṃ kṣudram antarhitarathaṃ balātc rākṣasaṃ nihaniṣyanti dṛṣṭvā vānarayūthapāḥa yady eṣa bhūmiṃ viśate divaṃ vārasātalaṃ vāpi nabhastalaṃ vāc evaṃ nigūḍho pi mamāstradagdhaḥpatiṣyate bhūmitale gatāsuḥa ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ mahātmāraghupravīraḥ plavagarṣabhair vṛtaḥc vadhāya raudrasya nṛśaṃsakarmaṇastadā mahātmā tvaritaṃ nirīkṣatea vijñāya tu manas tasya rāghavasya mahātmanaḥc saṃnivṛtyāhavāt tasmāt praviveśa puraṃ tataḥa so nusmṛtya vadhaṃ teṣāṃ rākṣasānāṃ tarasvināmc krodhatāmrekṣaṇaḥ śūro nirjagāma mahādyutiḥa sa paścimena dvāreṇa niryayau rākṣasair vṛtaḥc indrajit tu mahāvīryaḥ paulastyo devakaṇṭakaḥa indrajit tu tato dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇauc raṇāyābhyudyatau vīrau māyāṃ prāduṣkarot tadāa indrajit tu rathe sthāpya sītāṃ māyāmayīṃ tadāc balena mahatāvṛtya tasyā vadham arocayata mohanārthaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ buddhiṃ kṛtvā sudurmatiḥc hantuṃ sītāṃ vyavasito vānarābhimukho yayaua taṃ dṛṣṭvā tv abhiniryāntaṃ nagaryāḥ kānanaukasaḥc utpetur abhisaṃkruddhāḥ śilāhastā yuyutsavaḥa hanūmān puratas teṣāṃ jagāma kapikuñjaraḥc pragṛhya sumahac chṛṅgaṃ parvatasya durāsadama sa dadarśa hatānandāṃ sītām indrajito rathec ekaveṇīdharāṃ dīnām upavāsakṛśānanāma parikliṣṭaikavasanām amṛjāṃ rāghavapriyāmc rajomalābhyām āliptaiḥ sarvagātrair varastriyama tāṃ nirīkṣya muhūrtaṃ tu maithilīm adhyavasya cac bāṣpaparyākulamukho hanūmān vyathito bhavata abravīt tāṃ tu śokārtāṃ nirānandāṃ tapasvināmc dṛṣṭvā rathe stitāṃ sītāṃ rākṣasendrasutāśritāma kiṃ samarthitam asyeti cintayan sa mahākapiḥc saha tair vānaraśreṣṭhair abhyadhāvata rāvaṇima tad vānarabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇiḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc kṛtvā viśokaṃ nistriṃśaṃ mūrdhni sītāṃ parāmṛśata taṃ striyaṃ paśyatāṃ teṣāṃ tāḍayām āsa rāvaṇiḥc krośantīṃ rāma rāmeti māyayā yojitāṃ rathea gṛhītamūrdhajāṃ dṛṣṭvā hanūmān dainyam āgataḥc duḥkhajaṃ vārinetrābhyām utsṛjan mārutātmajaḥe abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ krodhād rakṣodhipātmajama durātmann ātmanāśāya keśapakṣe parāmṛśaḥc brahmarṣīṇāṃ kule jāto rākṣasīṃ yonim āśritaḥe dhik tvāṃ pāpasamācāraṃ yasya te matir īdṛśīa nṛśaṃsānārya durvṛtta kṣudra pāpaparākramac anāryasyedṛśaṃ karma ghṛṇā te nāsti nirghṛṇaa cyutā gṛhāc ca rājyāc ca rāmahastāc ca maithilīc kiṃ tavaiṣāparāddhā hi yad enāṃ hantum icchasia sītāṃ ca hatvā na ciraṃ jīviṣyasi kathaṃ canac vadhārhakarmaṇānena mama hastagato hy asia ye ca strīghātināṃ lokā lokavadhyaiś ca kutsitāḥc iha jīvitam utsṛjya pretya tān pratilapsyasea iti bruvāṇo hanumān sāyudhair haribhir vṛtaḥc abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho rākṣasendrasutaṃ pratia āpatantaṃ mahāvīryaṃ tad anīkaṃ vanaukasāmc rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānām anīkena nyavārayata sa tāṃ bāṇasahasreṇa vikṣobhya harivāhinīmc hariśreṣṭhaṃ hanūmantam indrajit pratyuvāca haa sugrīvas tvaṃ ca rāmaś ca yannimittam ihāgatāḥc tāṃ haniṣyāmi vaidehīm adyaiva tava paśyataḥa imāṃ hatvā tato rāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ tvāṃ ca vānarac sugrīvaṃ ca vadhiṣyāmi taṃ cānāryaṃ vibhīṣaṇama na hantavyāḥ striyaś ceti yad bravīṣi plavaṃgamac pīḍā karam amitrāṇāṃ yat syāt kartavyam eta tata tam evam uktvā rudatīṃ sītāṃ māyāmayīṃ tataḥc śitadhāreṇa khaḍgena nijaghānendrajit svayama yajñopavītamārgeṇa chinnā tena tapasvinīc sā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthuśroṇī papāta priyadarśanāa tām indrajitstriyaṃ hatvā hanūmantam uvāca hac mayā rāmasya paśyemāṃ kopena ca niṣūditāma tataḥ khaḍgena mahatā hatvā tām indrajit svayamc hṛṣṭaḥ sa ratham āsthāya vinanāda mahāsvanama vānarāḥ śuśruvuḥ śabdam adūre pratyavasthitāḥc vyāditāsyasya nadatas tad durgaṃ saṃśritasya tua tathā tu sītāṃ vinihatya durmatiḥprahṛṣṭacetāḥ sa babhūva rāvaṇiḥc taṃ hṛṣṭarūpaṃ samudīkṣya vānarāviṣaṇṇarūpāḥ samabhipradudruvuḥa śrutvā taṃ bhīmanirhrādaṃ śakrāśanisamasvanamc vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ sarvā dudruvur vānararṣabhāḥa tān uvāca tataḥ sarvān hanūmān mārutātmajaḥc viṣaṇṇavadanān dīnāṃs trastān vidravataḥ pṛthaka kasmād viṣaṇṇavadanā vidravadhvaṃ plavaṃgamāḥc tyaktayuddhasamutsāhāḥ śūratvaṃ kva nu vo gatama pṛṣṭhato nuvrajadhvaṃ mām agrato yāntam āhavec śūrair abhijanopetair ayuktaṃ hi nivartituma evam uktāḥ susaṃkruddhā vāyuputreṇa dhīmatāc śailaśṛṅgān drumāṃś caiva jagṛhur hṛṣṭamānasāḥa abhipetuś ca garjanto rākṣasān vānararṣabhāḥc parivārya hanūmantam anvayuś ca mahāhavea sa tair vānaramukhyais tu hanūmān sarvato vṛtaḥc hutāśana ivārciṣmān adahac chatruvāhinīma sa rākṣasānāṃ kadanaṃ cakāra sumahākapiḥc vṛto vānarasainyena kālāntakayamopamaḥa sa tu śokena cāviṣṭaḥ krodhena ca mahākapiḥc hanūmān rāvaṇi rathe mahatīṃ pātayac chilāma tām āpatantīṃ dṛṣṭvaiva rathaḥ sārathinā tadāc vidheyāśva samāyuktaḥ sudūram apavāhitaḥa tam indrajitam aprāpya rathathaṃ sahasārathimc viveśa dharaṇīṃ bhittvā sā śilāvyartham udyatāa patitāyāṃ śilāyāṃ tu rakṣasāṃ vyathitā camūḥc tam abhyadhāvañ śataśo nadantaḥ kānanaukasaḥa te drumāṃś ca mahākāyā giriśṛṅgāṇi codyatāḥc cikṣipur dviṣatāṃ madhye vānarā bhīmavikramāḥa vānarair tair mahāvīryair ghorarūpā niśācarāḥc vīryād abhihatā vṛkṣair vyaveṣṭanta raṇakṣitaua svasainyam abhivīkṣyātha vānarārditam indrajitc pragṛhītāyudhaḥ kruddhaḥ parān abhimukho yayaua sa śaraughān avasṛjan svasainyenābhisaṃvṛtaḥc jaghāna kapiśārdūlān subahūn dṛṣṭavikramaḥa śūlair aśanibhiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paṭṭasaiḥ kūṭamudgaraiḥc te cāpy anucarāṃs tasya vānarā jaghnur āhavea saskandhaviṭapaiḥ sālaiḥ śilābhiś ca mahābalaiḥc hanūmān kadanaṃ cakre rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāma sa nivārya parānīkam abravīt tān vanaukasaḥc hanūmān saṃnivartadhvaṃ na naḥ sādhyam idaṃ balama tyaktvā prāṇān viceṣṭanto rāma priyacikīrṣavaḥc yannimittaṃ hi yudhyāmo hatā sā janakātmajāa imam arthaṃ hi vijñāpya rāmaṃ sugrīvam eva cac tau yat pratividhāsyete tat kariṣyāmahe vayama ity uktvā vānaraśreṣṭho vārayan sarvavānarānc śanaiḥ śanair asaṃtrastaḥ sabalaḥ sa nyavartataa sa tu prekṣya hanūmantaṃ vrajantaṃ yatra rāghavaḥc nikumbhilām adhiṣṭhāya pāvakaṃ juhuve ndrajita yajñabhūmyāṃ tu vidhivat pāvakas tena rakṣasāc hūyamānaḥ prajajvāla homaśoṇitabhuk tadāa so rciḥ pinaddho dadṛśe homaśoṇitatarpitaḥc saṃdhyāgata ivādityaḥ sa tīvrāgniḥ samutthitaḥa athendrajid rākṣasabhūtaye tujuhāva havyaṃ vidhinā vidhānavatc dṛṣṭvā vyatiṣṭhanta ca rākṣasās temahāsamūheṣu nayānayajñāḥa rāghavaś cāpi vipulaṃ taṃ rākṣasavanaukasāmc śrutvā saṃgrāmanirghoṣaṃ jāmbavantam uvāca haa saumya nūnaṃ hanumatā kṛtaṃ karma suduṣkaramc śrūyate hi yathā bhīmaḥ sumahān āyudhasvanaḥa tad gaccha kuru sāhāyyaṃ svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥc kṣipram ṛṣkapate tasya kapiśreṣṭhasya yudhyataḥa ṛkṣarājas tathety uktvā svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥc āgacchat paścimadvāraṃ hanūmān yatra vānaraḥa athāyāntaṃ hanūmantaṃ dadarśarkṣapatiḥ pathic vānaraiḥ kṛtasaṃgrāmaiḥ śvasadbhir abhisaṃvṛtama dṛṣṭvā pathi hanūmāṃś ca tad ṛṣkabalam udyatamc nīlameghanibhaṃ bhīmaṃ saṃnivārya nyavartataa sa tena harisainyena saṃnikarṣaṃ mahāyaśāḥc śīghram āgamya rāmāya duḥkhito vākyam abravīta samare yudhyamānānām asmākaṃ prekṣatāṃ ca saḥc jaghāna rudatīṃ sītām indrajid rāvaṇātmajaḥa udbhrāntacittas tāṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣaṇṇo ham ariṃdamac tad ahaṃ bhavato vṛttaṃ vijñāpayitum āgataḥa tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavaḥ śokamūrchitaḥc nipapāta tadā bhūmau chinnamūla iva drumaḥa taṃ bhūmau devasaṃkāśaṃ patitaṃ dṛśya rāghavamc abhipetuḥ samutpatya sarvataḥ kapisattamāḥa asiñcan salilaiś cainaṃ padmotpalasugandhibhiḥc pradahantam asahyaṃ ca sahasāgnim ivotthitama taṃ lakṣmaṇo tha bāhubhyāṃ pariṣvajya suduḥkhitaḥc uvāca rāmam asvasthaṃ vākyaṃ hetvarthasaṃhitama śubhe vartmani tiṣṭhantaṃ tvām āryavijitendriyamc anarthebhyo na śaknoti trātuṃ dharmo nirarthakaḥa bhūtānāṃ sthāvarāṇāṃ ca jaṅgamānāṃ ca darśanamc yathāsti na tathā dharmas tena nāstīti me matiḥa yathaiva sthāvaraṃ vyaktaṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca tathāvidhamc nāyam arthas tathā yuktas tvadvidho na vipadyatea yady adharmo bhaved bhūto rāvaṇo narakaṃ vrajetc bhavāṃś ca dharmasaṃyukto naivaṃ vyasanam āpnuyāta tasya ca vyasanābhāvād vyasanaṃ ca gate tvayic dharmeṇopalabhed dharmam adharmaṃ cāpy adharmataḥa yadi dharmeṇa yujyeran nādharmarucayo janāḥc dharmeṇa caratāṃ dharmas tathā caiṣāṃ phalaṃ bhaveta yasmād arthā vivardhante yeṣv adharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥc kliśyante dharmaśīlāś ca tasmād etau nirarthakaua vadhyante pāpakarmāṇo yady adharmeṇa rāghavac vadhakarmahato dharmaḥ sa hataḥ kaṃ vadhiṣyatia atha vā vihitenāyaṃ hanyate hanti vā paramc vidhir ālipyate tena na sa pāpena karmaṇāa adṛṣṭapratikāreṇa avyaktenāsatā satāc kathaṃ śakyaṃ paraṃ prāptuṃ dharmeṇārivikarśanaa yadi sat syāt satāṃ mukhya nāsat syāt tava kiṃ canac tvayā yadīdṛśaṃ prāptaṃ tasmāt san nopapadyatea atha vā durbalaḥ klībo balaṃ dharmo nuvartatec durbalo hṛtamaryādo na sevya iti me matiḥa balasya yadi ced dharmo guṇabhūtaḥ parākramec dharmam utsṛjya vartasva yathā dharme tathā balea atha cet satyavacanaṃ dharmaḥ kila paraṃtapac anṛtas tvayy akaruṇaḥ kiṃ na baddhas tvayā pitāa yadi dharmo bhaved bhūta adharmo vā paraṃtapac na sma hatvā muniṃ vajrī kuryād ijyāṃ śatakratuḥa adharmasaṃśrito dharmo vināśayati rāghavac sarvam etad yathākāmaṃ kākutstha kurute naraḥa mama cedaṃ mataṃ tāta dharmo yam iti rāghavac dharmamūlaṃ tvayā chinnaṃ rājyam utsṛjatā tadāa arthebhyo hi vivṛddhebhyaḥ saṃvṛddhebhyas tatas tataḥc kriyāḥ sarvāḥ pravartante parvatebhya ivāpagāḥa arthena hi viyuktasya puruṣasyālpatejasaḥc vyucchidyante kriyāḥ sarvā grīṣme kusarito yathāa so yam arthaṃ parityajya sukhakāmaḥ sukhaidhitaḥc pāpam ārabhate kartuṃ tathā doṣaḥ pravartatea yasyārthās tasya mitrāṇi yasyārthās tasya bāndhavaḥc yasyārthāḥ sa pumāṃl loke yasyārthāḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥa yasyārthāḥ sa ca vikrānto yasyārthāḥ sa ca buddhimānc yasyārthāḥ sa mahābhāgo yasyārthāḥ sa mahāguṇaḥa arthasyaite parityāge doṣāḥ pravyāhṛtā mayāc rājyam utsṛjatā vīra yena buddhis tvayā kṛtāa yasyārthā dharmakāmārthās tasya sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇamc adhanenārthakāmena nārthaḥ śakyo vicinvatāa harṣaḥ kāmaś ca darpaś ca dharmaḥ krodhaḥ śamo damaḥc arthād etāni sarvāṇi pravartante narādhipaa yeṣāṃ naśyaty ayaṃ lokaś caratāṃ dharmacāriṇāmc te rthās tvayi na dṛśyante durdineṣu yathā grahāḥa tvayi pravrajite vīra guroś ca vacane sthitec rakṣasāpahṛtā bhāryā prāṇaiḥ priyatarā tavaa tad adya vipulaṃ vīra duḥkham indrajitā kṛtamc karmaṇā vyapaneṣyāmi tasmād uttiṣṭha rāghavaa ayam anagha tavoditaḥ priyārthaṃjanakasutā nidhanaṃ nirīkṣya ruṣṭaḥc sahayagajarathāṃ sarākṣasendrāṃbhṛśam iṣubhir vinipātayāmi laṅkāma rāmam āśvāsayāne tu lakṣmaṇe bhrātṛvatsalec nikṣipya gulmān svasthāne tatrāgacchad vibhīṣaṇaḥa nānāpraharaṇair vīraiś caturbhiḥ sacivair vṛtaḥc nīlāñjanacayākārair mātaṃgair iva yūthapaḥa so bhigamya mahātmānaṃ rāghavaṃ śokalālasaṃc vānarāṃś caiva dadṛśe bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇāna rāghavaṃ ca mahātmānam ikṣvākukulanandanamc dadarśa moham āpannaṃ lakṣmaṇasyāṅkam āśritama vrīḍitaṃ śokasaṃtaptaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥc antarduḥkhena dīnātmā kim etad iti so bravīta vibhīṣaṇa mukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvaṃ tāṃś ca vānarānc uvāca lakṣmaṇo vākyam idaṃ bāṣpapariplutaḥa hatām indrajitā sītām iha śrutvaiva rāghavaḥc hanūmad vacanāt saumya tato moham upāgataḥa kathayantaṃ tu saumitriṃ saṃnivārya vibhīṣaṇaḥc puṣkalārtham idaṃ vākyaṃ visaṃjñaṃ rāmam abravīta manujendrārtarūpeṇa yad uktas tvaṃ hanūmatāc tad ayuktam ahaṃ manye sāgarasyeva śoṣaṇama abhiprāyaṃ tu jānāmi rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥc sītāṃ prati mahābāho na ca ghātaṃ kariṣyatia yācyamānaḥ subahuśo mayā hitacikīrṣuṇāc vaidehīm utsṛjasveti na ca tat kṛtavān vacaḥa naiva sāmnā na bhedena na dānena kuto yudhāc sā draṣṭum api śakyeta naiva cānyena kena cita vānarān mohayitvā tu pratiyātaḥ sa rākṣasaḥc caityaṃ nikumbhilāṃ nāma yatra homaṃ kariṣyatia hutavān upayāto hi devair api savāsavaiḥc durādharṣo bhavaty eṣa saṃgrāme rāvaṇātmajaḥa tena mohayatā nūnam eṣā māyā prayojitāc vighnam anvicchatā tāta vānarāṇāṃ parākramee sasainyās tatra gacchāmo yāvat tan na samāpyatea tyajemaṃ naraśārdūlamithyā saṃtāpam āgatamc sīdate hi balaṃ sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā tvāṃ śokakarśitama iha tvaṃ svastha hṛdayas tiṣṭha sattvasamucchritaḥc lakṣmaṇaṃ preṣayāsmābhiḥ saha sainyānukarṣibhiḥa eṣa taṃ naraśārdūlo rāvaṇiṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc tyājayiṣyati tat karma tato vadhyo bhaviṣyatia tasyaite niśitās tīkṣṇāḥ patripatrāṅgavājinaḥc patatriṇa ivāsaumyāḥ śarāḥ pāsyanti śoṇitama tat saṃdiśa mahābāho lakṣmaṇaṃ śubhalakṣaṇamc rākṣasasya vināśāya vajraṃ vajradharo yathāa manujavara na kālaviprakarṣoripunidhanaṃ prati yat kṣamo dya kartumc tvam atisṛja ripor vadhāya bāṇīmasurapuronmathane yathā mahendraḥa samāptakarmā hi sa rākṣasendrobhavaty adṛśyaḥ samare surāsuraiḥc yuyutsatā tena samāptakarmaṇābhavet surāṇām api saṃśayo mahāna tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rāghavaḥ śokakarśitaḥc nopadhārayate vyaktaṃ yad uktaṃ tena rakṣasāa tato dhairyam avaṣṭabhya rāmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥc vibhīṣaṇam upāsīnam uvāca kapisaṃnidhaua nairṛtādhipate vākyaṃ yad uktaṃ te vibhīṣaṇac bhūyas tac chrotum icchāmi brūhi yat te vivakṣitama rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥc yat tat punar idaṃ vākyaṃ babhāṣe sa vibhīṣaṇaḥa yathājñaptaṃ mahābāho tvayā gulmaniveśanamc tat tathānuṣṭhitaṃ vīra tvadvākyasamanantarama tāny anīkāni sarvāṇi vibhaktāni samantataḥc vinyastā yūthapāś caiva yathānyāyaṃ vibhāgaśaḥa bhūyas tu mama vijāpyaṃ tac chṛṇuṣva mahāyaśaḥc tvayy akāraṇasaṃtapte saṃtaptahṛdayā vayama tyaja rājann imaṃ śokaṃ mithyā saṃtāpam āgatamc tad iyaṃ tyajyatāṃ cintā śatruharṣavivardhanīa udyamaḥ kriyatāṃ vīra harṣaḥ samupasevyatāmc prāptavyā yadi te sītā hantavyaś vca niśācarāḥa raghunandana vakṣyāmi śrūyatāṃ me hitaṃ vacaḥc sādhv ayaṃ yātu saumitrir balena mahatā vṛtaḥe nikumbhilāyāṃ saṃprāpya hantuṃ rāvaṇim āhavea dhanurmaṇḍalanirmuktair āśīviṣaviṣopamaiḥc śarair hantuṃ maheṣvāso rāvaṇiṃ samitiṃjayaḥa tena vīreṇa tapasā varadānāt svayambhutaḥc astraṃ brahmaśiraḥ prāptaṃ kāmagāś ca turaṃgamāḥa nikumbhilām asaṃprāptam ahutāgniṃ ca yo ripuḥc tvām ātatāyinaṃ hanyād indraśatro sa te vadhaḥe ity evaṃ vihito rājan vadhas tasyaiva dhīmataḥa vadhāyendrajito rāma taṃ diśasva mahābalamc hate tasmin hataṃ viddhi rāvaṇaṃ sasuhṛjjanama vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutva rāmo vākyam athābravītc jānāmi tasya raudrasya māyāṃ satyaparākramaa sa hi brahmāstravit prājño mahāmāyo mahābalaḥc karoty asaṃjñān saṃgrāme devān savaruṇān apia tasyāntarikṣe carato rathasthasya mahāyaśaḥc na gatir jñāyate vīrasūryasyevābhrasaṃplavea rāghavas tu ripor jñātvā māyāvīryaṃ durātmanaḥc lakṣmaṇaṃ kīrtisaṃpannam idaṃ vacanam abravīta yad vānarendrasya balaṃ tena sarveṇa saṃvṛtaḥc hanūmatpramukhaiś caiva yūthapaiḥ sahalakṣmaṇaa jāmbavenarkṣapatinā saha sainyena saṃvṛtaḥc jahi taṃ rākṣasasutaṃ māyābalaviśāradama ayaṃ tvāṃ sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ mahātmā rajanīcaraḥc abhijñas tasya deśasya pṛṣṭhato nugamiṣyatia rāghavasya vacaḥ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥc jagrāha kārmukaṃ śreṣṭham anyad bhīmaparākramaḥa saṃnaddhaḥ kavacī khaḍgī sa śarī hemacāpadhṛkc rāmapādāv upaspṛśya hṛṣṭaḥ saumitrir abravīta adya matkārmukonmukhāḥ śarā nirbhidya rāvaṇimc laṅkām abhipatiṣyanti haṃsāḥ puṣkariṇīm ivaa adyaiva tasya raudrasya śarīraṃ māmakāḥ śarāḥc vidhamiṣyanti hatvā taṃ mahācāpaguṇacyutāḥa sa evam uktvā dyutimān vacanaṃ bhrātur agrataḥc sa rāvaṇivadhākāṅkṣī lakṣmaṇas tvarito yayaua so bhivādya guroḥ pādau kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇamc nikumbhilām abhiyayau caityaṃ rāvaṇipālitama vibhīṣaṇena sahito rājaputraḥ pratāpavānc kṛtasvastyayano bhrātrā lakṣmaṇas tvarito yayaua vānarāṇāṃ sahasrais tu hanūmān bahubhir vṛtaḥc vibhīṣaṇaḥ sahāmātyas tadā lakṣmaṇam anvagāta mahatā harisainyena savegam abhisaṃvṛtaḥc ṛkṣarājabalaṃ caiva dadarśa pathi viṣṭhitama sa gatvā dūram adhvānaṃ saumitrir mitranandanaḥc rākṣasendrabalaṃ dūrād apaśyad vyūham āsthitama sa saṃprāpya dhanuṣpāṇir māyāyogam ariṃdamac tasthau brahmavidhānena vijetuṃ raghunandanaḥa vividham amalaśastrabhāsvaraṃ taddhvajagahanaṃ vipulaṃ mahārathaiś cac pratibhayatamam aprameyavegaṃtimiram iva dviṣatāṃ balaṃ viveśaa atha tasyām avasthāyāṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ rāvaṇānujaḥc pareṣām ahitaṃ vākyam arthasādhakam abravīta asyānīkasya mahato bhedane yatalakṣmaṇac rākṣasendrasuto py atra bhinne dṛśyo bhaviṣyatia sa tvam indrāśaniprakhyaiḥ śarair avakiran parānc abhidravāśu yāvad vai naitat karma samāpyatea jahi vīradurātmānaṃ māyāparam adhārmikamc rāvaṇiṃ krūrakarmāṇaṃ sarvalokabhayāvahama vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ śrutvā lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi rākṣasendrasutaṃ pratia ṛkṣāḥ śākhāmṛgāś caiva drumādrivarayodhinaḥc abhyadhāvanta sahitās tad anīkam avasthitama rākṣasāś ca śitair bāṇair asibhiḥ śaktitomaraiḥc udyataiḥ samavartanta kapisainyajighāṃsavaḥa sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ saṃjajñe kapirakṣasāmc śabdena mahatā laṅkāṃ nādayan vai samantataḥa śastrair bahuvidhākāraiḥ śitair bāṇaiś ca pādapaiḥc udyatair giriśṛṅgaiś ca ghorair ākāśam āvṛtama te rākṣasā vānareṣu vikṛtānanabāhavaḥc niveśayantaḥ śastrāṇi cakrus te sumahad bhayama tathaiva sakalair vṛkṣair giriśṛṅgaiś ca vānarāḥc abhijaghnur nijaghnuś ca samare rākṣasarṣabhāna ṛkṣavānaramukhyaiś ca mahākāyair mahābalaiḥc rakṣasāṃ vadhyamānānāṃ mahad bhayam ajāyataa svam anīkaṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ tu śrutvā śatrubhir arditamc udatiṣṭhata durdharṣas tat karmaṇy ananuṣṭhitea vṛkṣāndhakārān niṣkramya jātakrodhaḥ sa rāvaṇiḥc āruroha rathaṃ sajjaṃ pūrvayuktaṃ sa rākṣasaḥa sa bhīmakārmukaśaraḥ kṛṣṇāñjanacayopamaḥc raktāsyanayanaḥ krūro babhau mṛtyur ivāntakaḥa dṛṣṭvaiva tu rathasthaṃ taṃ paryavartata tad balamc rakṣasāṃ bhīmavegānāṃ lakṣmaṇena yuyutsatāma tasmin kāle tu hanumān udyamya sudurāsadamc dharaṇīdharasaṃkāśī mahāvṛkṣam ariṃdamaḥa sa rākṣasānāṃ tat sainyaṃ kālāgnir iva nirdahanc cakāra bahubhir vṛkṣair niḥsaṃjñaṃ yudhi vānaraḥa vidhvaṃsayantaṃ tarasā dṛṣṭvaiva pavanātmajamc rākṣasānāṃ sahasrāṇi hanūmantam avākirana śitaśūladharāḥ śūlair asibhiś cāsipāṇayaḥc śaktibhiḥ śaktihastāś ca paṭṭasaiḥ paṭṭasāyudhāḥa parighaiś ca gadābhiś ca kuntaiś ca śubhadarśanaiḥc śataśaś ca śataghnībhir āyasair api mudgaraiḥa ghoraiḥ paraśubhiś caiva bhiṇḍipālaiś ca rākṣasāḥc muṣṭibhir vajravegaiś ca talair aśanisaṃnibhaiḥa abhijaghnuḥ samāsādya samantāt parvatopamamc teṣām api ca saṃkruddhaś cakāra kadanaṃ mahata sa dadarśa kapiśreṣṭham acalopamam indrajitc sūdayānam amitraghnam amitrān pavanātmajama sa sārathim uvācedaṃ yāhi yatraiṣa vānaraḥc kṣayam eva hi naḥ kuryād rākṣasānām upekṣitaḥa ity uktaḥ sārathis tena yayau yatra sa mārutiḥc vahan paramadurdharṣaṃ sthitam indrajitaṃ rathea so bhyupetya śarān khaḍgān paṭṭasāsiparaśvadhānc abhyavarṣata durdharṣaḥ kapimūrdhni sa rākṣasaḥa tāni śastrāṇi ghorāṇi pratigṛhya sa mārutiḥc roṣeṇa mahatāviṣo vākyaṃ cedam uvāca haa yudhyasva yadi śūro si rāvaṇātmaja durmatec vāyuputraṃ samāsādya na jīvan pratiyāsyasia bāhubhyāṃ saṃprayudhyasva yadi me dvandvam āhavec vegaṃ sahasva durbuddhe tatas tvaṃ rakṣasāṃ varaḥa hanūmantaṃ jighāṃsantaṃ samudyataśarāsanamc rāvaṇātmajam ācaṣṭe lakṣmaṇāya vibhīṣaṇaḥa yas tu vāsavanirjetā rāvaṇasyātmasaṃbhavaḥc sa eṣa ratham āsthāya hanūmantaṃ jighāṃsatia tam apratimasaṃsthānaiḥ śaraiḥ śatruvidāraṇaiḥc jīvitāntakarair ghoraiḥ saumitre rāvaṇiṃ jahia ity evam uktas tu tadā mahātmāvibhīṣaṇenārivibhīṣaṇenac dadarśa taṃ parvatasaṃnikāśaṃrathasthitaṃ bhīmabalaṃ durāsadama evam uktvā tu saumitriṃ jātaharṣo vibhīṣaṇaḥc dhanuṣpāṇinam ādāya tvaramāṇo jagāma saḥa avidūraṃ tato gatvā praviśya ca mahad vanamc darśayām āsa tat karma lakṣmaṇāya vibhīṣaṇaḥa nīlajīmūtasaṃkāśaṃ nyagrodhaṃ bhīmadarśanamc tejasvī rāvaṇabhrātā lakṣmaṇāya nyavedayata ihopahāraṃ bhūtānāṃ balavān rāvaṇātajaḥc upahṛtya tataḥ paścāt saṃgrāmam abhivartatea adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati rākṣasaḥc nihanti samare śatrūn badhnāti ca śarottamaiḥa tam apraviṣṭaṃ nyagrodhaṃ balinaṃ rāvaṇātmajamc vidhvaṃsaya śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ sarathaṃ sāśvasārathima tathety uktvā mahātejāḥ saumitrir mitranandanaḥc babhūvāvasthitas tatra citraṃ visphārayan dhanuḥa sa rathenāgnivarṇena balavān rāvaṇātmajaḥc indrajit kavacī khaḍgī sadhvajaḥ pratyadṛśyataa tam uvāca mahātejāḥ paulastyam aparājitamc samāhvaye tvāṃ samare samyag yuddhaṃ prayaccha mea evam ukto mahātejā manasvī rāvaṇātmajaḥc abravīt paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā vibhīṣaṇama iha tvaṃ jātasaṃvṛddhaḥ sākṣād bhrātā pitur mamac kathaṃ druhyasi putrasya pitṛvyo mama rākṣasaa na jñātitvaṃ na sauhārdaṃ na jātis tava durmatec pramāṇaṃ na ca sodaryaṃ na dharmo dharmadūṣaṇaa śocyas tvam asi durbuddhe nindanīyaś ca sādhubhiḥc yas tvaṃ svajanam utsṛjya parabhṛtyatvam āgataḥa naitac chithilayā buddhyā tvaṃ vetsi mahad antaramc kva ca svajanasaṃvāsaḥ kva ca nīcaparāśrayaḥa guṇavān vā parajanaḥ svajano nirguṇo pi vāc nirguṇaḥ svajanaḥ śreyān yaḥ paraḥ para eva saḥa niranukrośatā ceyaṃ yādṛśī te niśācarac svajanena tvayā śakyaṃ paruṣaṃ rāvaṇānujaa ity ukto bhrātṛputreṇa pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥc ajānann iva macchīlaṃ kiṃ rākṣasa vikatthasea rākṣasendrasutāsādho pāruṣyaṃ tyaja gauravātc kule yady apy ahaṃ jāto rakṣasāṃ krūrakarmaṇāme guṇo yaṃ prathamo nṝṇāṃ tan me śīlam arākṣasaṃa na rame dāruṇenāhaṃ na cādharmeṇa vai ramec bhrātrā viṣamaśīlena kathaṃ bhrātā nirasyatea parasvānāṃ ca haraṇaṃ paradārābhimarśanamc suhṛdām atiśaṅkāṃ ca trayo doṣāḥ kṣayāvahāḥa maharṣīṇāṃ vadho ghoraḥ sarvadevaiś ca vigrahaḥc abhimānaś ca kopaś ca vairitvaṃ pratikūlatāa ete doṣā mama sthitaḥ kālāntakopamaḥa mahāpramāṇam udyamya vipulaṃ vegavad dṛḍhamc dhanur bhīmaṃ parāmṛśya śarāṃś cāmitranāśanāna uvācainaṃ samārabdhaḥ saumitriṃ savibhīṣaṇamc tāṃś ca vānaraśārdūlān paśyadhvaṃ me parākramama adya matkārmukotsṛṣṭaṃ śaravarṣaṃ durāsadamc muktaṃ varṣam ivākāśe vārayiṣyatha saṃyugea adya vo māmakā bāṇā mahākārmukaniḥsṛtāḥc vidhamiṣyanti gātrāṇi tūlarāśim ivānalaḥa rākṣasendrasya garjitaṃ lakṣmaṇas tadāc abhītavadanaḥ kruddho rāvaṇiṃ vākyam abravīta uktaś ca durgamaḥ pāraḥ kāryāṇāṃ rākṣasa tvayāc kāryāṇāṃ karmaṇā pāraṃ yo gacchati sa buddhimāna sa tvam arthasya lakṣmaṇaṃ petuḥ śvasanta iva pannagāḥa śarair atimahāvegair vegavān rāvaṇātmajaḥc saumitrim indrajid yuddhe vivyādha śubhalakṣaṇama sa śarair atividdhāṅgo rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥc śuśubhe lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān vidhūma iva pāvakaḥa indrajit tv ātmanaḥ karma prasamīkṣyādhigamya cac vinadya sumahānādam idaṃ vacanam abravīta patriṇaḥ śitadhārās te śarā matkārmukacyutāḥc ādāsyante dya saumitre jīvitaṃ jīvitāntagāḥa adya gomāyusaṃghāś ca śyenasaṃghāś ca lakṣmaṇac gṛdhrāś ca nipatantu tvāṃ gatāsuṃ nihataṃ mayāa kṣatrabandhuḥ sadānāryo rāmaḥ paramadurmatiḥc bhaktaṃ bhrātaram adyaiva tvāṃ drakṣyati mayā hatama viśastakavacaṃ bhūmau vyapaviddhaśarāsanamc hṛtottamāṅgaṃ saumitre tvām adya nihataṃ mayāa iti bruvāṇaṃ saṃrabdhaṃ paruṣaṃ rāvaṇātmajamc hetumadvākyam atyarthaṃ lakṣmaṇaḥ pratyuvāca haa saṃdhāyāmitrakarśanaḥc sasarja rākṣasendrāya kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasana tasya jyātalanirghoṣaṃ sa śrutvā rāvaṇātmajaḥc vivarṇavadano bhūtvā lakṣmaṇaṃ samudaikṣataa taṃ viṣaṇṇamukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasaṃ rāvaṇātmajamc saumitriṃ yuddhasaṃsaktaṃ pratyuvāca vibhīṣaṇaḥa nimittāny anupaśyāmi yāny asmin rāvaṇātmajec tvara tena mahābāho bhagna eṣa na saṃśayaḥa tataḥ saṃdhāya saumitriḥ śarān agniśikhopamānc mumoca niśitāṃs tasmai sarvān iva viṣolbaṇāna śakrāśanisamasparśair lakṣmaṇenāhataḥ śaraiḥc muhūrtam abhavan mūḍhaḥ sarvasaṃkṣubhitendriyaḥa upalabhya muhūrtena saṃjñāṃ pratyāgatendriyaḥc dadarśāvasthitaṃ vīraṃ vīro daśarathātmajama so bhicakrāma saumitriṃ roṣāt saṃraktalocanaḥc abravīc cainam āsādya punaḥ sa paruṣaṃ vacaḥa kiṃ na smarasi tad yuddhe prathame matparākramamc nibaddhas yasmāt tvaṃ māṃ dharṣayitum icchasia yadi te prathame yuddhe na dṛṣṭo matparākramaḥc adya tvāṃ darśayiṣyāmi tiṣṭhedānīṃ vyavasthitaḥa ity uktvā saptabhir bāṇair abhivivyādha lakṣmaṇamc daśabhiś ca pṛthakpṛthag bhīmaḥ śuśruve talanisvanaḥc sughorayor niṣṭanator gagane meghayor ivaa te gātrayor nipatitā rukmapuṅkhāḥ śarā yudhic asṛgdigdhā viniṣpetur viviśur dharaṇītalama anyaiḥ suniśitaiḥ babhrājuḥ sarvagātrāṇi jvalanta iva pāvakāḥa tayor atha mahān kālo vyatīyād yudhyamānayoḥc na ca tau yuddhavaimukhyaṃ śramaṃ vāpy upajagmatuḥa atha samarapariśramaṃ nihantuṃsamaramukheṣv ajitasya śamayiṣyatie vānarā ghnantuṃ saṃbhūya bhṛtyān asya samīpagāna iti tenātiyaśasā rākṣasenābhicoditāḥc vānarendrā jahṛṣire lāṅgalāni ca vivyadhuḥa tatas te kapiśārdūlāḥ kṣveḍantaś ca muhur muhuḥc mumucur tejasāa tau dhanvinau jighāṃsantāv anyonyam iṣubhir bhṛśamc vijayenābhiniṣkrāntau vane gajavṛṣāv ivaa nibarhayantaś cānyonyaṃ te rākṣasavanaukasaḥc bhartāraṃ na jahur yuddhe saṃpatantas tatas tataḥa sa lakṣmaṇaṃ samuddiśya paraṃ lāghavam āsthitaḥc vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi varṣāṇīva puraṃdaraḥa muktam indrajitā tat tu śaravarṣam ariṃdamaḥc avārayad asaṃbhrānto lakṣmaṇaḥ sudurāsadama abhedyakacanaṃ matvā lakṣmaṇaṃ rāvaṇātmajaḥc lalāṭe lakṣmaṇaṃ bāṇaiḥ supuṅkhais tribhir indrajite avidhyat paramakruddhaḥ śīghram astraṃ pradarśayana taiḥ pṛṣatkair lalāṭasthaiḥ śuśubhe raghunandanaḥc raṇāgre mahābalaḥa taṃ samīkṣya mahātejā maheṣuṃ tena saṃhitamc lakṣmaṇo py ādade bāṇam anyaṃ bhīmaparākramaḥa kubereṇa svayaṃ svapne yad dattam amitātmanāc durjayaṃ durviṣahyaṃ ca sendrair api surāsuraiḥa saumitrir astraṃ vāruṇam ādadec raudraṃ mahedrajid yuddhe vyasṛjad yudhi viṣṭhitaḥa tayoḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃbabhūvādbhutopamamc gaganasthāni bhūtāni lakṣmaṇaṃ paryavārayana bhairavābhirute bhīme yuddhe vānararākṣasāmc bhūtair bahubhir ākāśaṃ vismitair āvṛtaṃ babhaua ṛṣayaḥ pitaro devā gandharvā garuṇoragāḥc śatakratuṃ puraskṛtya rarakṣur lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇea athānyaṃ mārgaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ saṃdadhe rāvaṇānujaḥc hutāśanasamasparśaṃ rāvaṇātmajadāruṇama supatram anuvṛttāṅgaṃ suparvāṇaṃ susaṃsthitamc suvarṇavikṛtaṃ vīraḥ śarīrāntakaraṃ śarama durāvāraṃ durviṣahaṃ rākṣasānāṃ bhayāvahamc āśīviṣaviṣaprakhyaṃ devasaṃghaiḥ samarcitama yena śakro mahātejā dānavān ajayat prabhuḥc purā devāsure yuddhe vīryavān harivāhanaḥa tad aindram astraṃ saumitriḥ saṃyugeṣv aparājitamc śaraśreṣṭhaṃ dhanuḥ śreṣṭhe naraśreṣṭho bhisaṃdadhea saṃdhāyāmitradalanaṃ vicakarṣa śarāsanamc sajyam āyamya durdharśaḥ kālo lokakṣaye yathāa saṃdhāya dhanuṣi śreṣṭhe vikarṣann idam abravītc lakṣmīvāṃl lakṣmaṇo vākyam arthasādhakam ātmanaḥa dharmātmā satyasaṃdhaś ca rāmo dāśarathir yadic pauruṣe cāpratidvandvas tad enaṃ jahi rāvaṇima ity uktvā bāṇam ākarṇaṃ vikṛṣya tam ajihmagamc lakṣmaṇaḥ samare vīraḥ sasarjendrajitaṃ pratie aindrāstreṇa samāyujya lakṣmaṇaḥ paravīrahāa tac chiraḥ saśiras trāṇaṃ śrīmaj jvalitakuṇḍalamc pramathyendrajitaḥ kāyāt papāta dharaṇītalea tad rākṣasatanūjasya chinnaskandhaṃ śiro mahatc tapanīyanibhaṃ bhūmau dadṛśe rudhirokṣitama hatas tu nipapātāśu dharaṇyāṃ rāvaṇātmajaḥc kavacī saśirastrāṇo vidhvastaḥ saśarāsanaḥa cukruśus te tataḥ sarve vānarāḥ savibhīṣaṇāḥc hṛṣyanto nihate tasmin devā vṛtravadhe yathāa athāntarikṣe bhūtānām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca mahātmanāmc abhijajñe ca saṃnādo gandharvāpsarasām apia patitaṃ samabhijñāya rākṣasī sā mahācamūḥc vadhyamānā diśo bheje haribhir jitakāśibhiḥa vanarair vadhyamānās te śastrāṇy utsṛjya rākṣasāḥc laṅkām abhimukhāḥ sarve naṣṭasaṃjñāḥ pradhāvitāḥa dudruvur bahudhā bhītā rākṣasāḥ śataśo diśaḥc tyaktvā praharaṇān sarve paṭṭasāsiparaśvadhāna ke cil laṅkāṃ paritrastāḥ praviṣṭā vānarārditāḥc samudre patitāḥ ke cit ke cit parvatam āśritāḥa hatam indrajitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānaṃ samarakṣitauc rākṣasānāṃ sahasreṣu na kaś cit pratyadṛśyataa yathāstaṃ gata āditye nāvatiṣṭhanti raśmayaḥc tathā tasmin nipatite rākṣasās te gatā diśaḥa śāntarakśmir ivādityo nirvāṇa iva pāvakaḥc sa babhūva mahātejā vyapāsta gatajīvitaḥa praśāntapīḍā bahulo vinaṣṭāriḥ praharṣavānc babhūva lokaḥ patite rākṣasendrasute tadāa harṣaṃ ca śakro bhagavān saha sarvaiḥ surarṣabhaiḥc jagāma nihate tasmin rākṣase pāpakarmaṇia śuddhā āpo nabhaś caiva jahṛṣur daityadānavāḥc ājagmuḥ patite tasmin sarvalokabhayāvahea ūcuś ca sahitāḥ sarve devagandharvadānavāḥc vijvarāḥ śāntakaluṣā brāhmaṇā vicarantv itia tato bhyanandan saṃhṛṣṭāḥ samare hariyūthapāḥc tam apratibalaṃ dṛṣṭvā hataṃ nairṛtapuṃgavama vibhīṣaṇo hanūmāṃś ca jāmbavāṃś carkṣayūthapaḥc vijayenābhinandantas tuṣṭuvuś cāpi lakṣmaṇama kṣveḍantaś ca nadantaś ca garjantaś ca plavaṃgamāḥc labdhalakṣā raghusutaṃ parivāryopatasthirea lāṅgūlāni pravidhyantaḥ sphoṭayantaś ca vānarāḥc lakṣmaṇo jayatīty evaṃ vākyaṃ vyaśrāvayaṃs tadāa anyonyaṃ ca samāśliṣya kapayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥc cakrur uccāvacaguṇā rāghavāśrayajāḥ kathāḥa tad asukaram athābhivīkṣya hṛṣṭāḥpriyasuhṛdo yudhi lakṣmaṇasya karmac paramam upalabhan manaḥpraharṣaṃvinihatam indraripuṃ niśamya devāḥa rudhiraklinnagātras tu lakṣmaṇaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥc babhūva hṛṣṭas taṃ hatvā śakrajetāram āhavea tataḥ sa jāmbavantaṃ ca hanūmantaṃ ca vīryavānc saṃnivartya mahātejās tāṃś ca sarvān vanaukasaḥa ājagāma tataḥ śīghraṃ yatra sugrīvarāghavauc vibhīṣaṇam avaṣṭabhya hanūmantaṃ ca lakṣmaṇaḥa tato rāmam abhikramya saumitrir abhivādya cac tasthau bhrātṛsamīpasthaḥ śakrasyendrānujo yathāe ācacakṣe tadā vīro ghoram indrajito vadhama rāvaṇas tu śiraś chinnaṃ lakṣmaṇena mahātmanāc nyavedayata rāmāya tadā hṛṣṭo vibhīṣaṇaḥa upaveśya tam utsaṅge pariṣvajyāvapīḍitamc mūrdhni cainam upāghrāya bhūyaḥ saṃspṛśya ca tvarane uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ vākyam āśvāsya puruṣarṣabhaḥa kṛtaṃ paramakalyāṇaṃ karma duṣkarakāriṇāc niramitraḥ kṛto smy adya niryāsyati hi rāvaṇaḥe balavyūhena mahatā śrutvā putraṃ nipātitama taṃ putravadhasaṃtaptaṃ niryāntaṃ rākṣasādhipamc balenāvṛtya mahatā nihaniṣyāmi durjayama tvayā lakṣmaṇa nāthena sītā ca pṛthivī ca mec na duṣprāpā hate tv adya śakrajetari cāhavea sa taṃ bhrātaram āśvāsya pāriṣvajya ca rāghavaḥc rāmaḥ suṣeṇaṃ muditaḥ samābhāṣyedam abravīta saśalyo yaṃ mahāprājñaḥ saumitrir mitravatsalaḥc yathā bhavati susvasthas tathā tvaṃ samupācarae viśalyaḥ kriyatāṃ kṣipraṃ saumitriḥ savibhīṣaṇaḥa kṛṣa vānarasainyānāṃ śūrāṇāṃ drumayodhināmc ye cānye tra ca yudhyantaḥ saśalyā vraṇinas tathāe te pi sarve prayatnena kriyantāṃ sukhinas tvayāa evam uktaḥ sa rāmeṇa mahātmā hariyūthapaḥc lakṣmaṇāya dadau nastaḥ suṣeṇaḥ paramauṣadhama sa tasya gandham āghrāya viśalyaḥ samapadyatac tadā nirvedanaś caiva saṃrūḍhavraṇa eva caa vibhīṣaṇa mukhānāṃ ca suhṛdāṃ rāghavājñayāc sarvavānaramukhyānāṃ cikitsāṃ sa tadākarota tataḥ prakṛtim āpanno hṛtaśalyo gatavyathaḥc saumitrir muditas tatra kṣaṇena vigatajvaraḥa tathaiva rāmaḥ plavagādhipas tadāvibhīṣaṇaś carkṣapatiś ca jāmbavānc avekṣya saumitrim arogam utthitaṃmudā sasainyaḥ suciraṃ jaharṣirea apūjayat karma sa lakṣmaṇasyasuduṣkaraṃ dāśarathir mahātmāc hṛṣṭā babhūvur yudhi yūthapendrāniśamya taṃ śakrajitaṃ nipātitama tataḥ paulastya sacivāḥ śrutvā cendrajitaṃ hatamc ācacakṣur abhijñāya daśagrīvāya savyathāḥa yuddhe hato mahārāja lakṣmaṇena tavātmajaḥc vibhīṣaṇasahāyena miṣatāṃ no mahādyutea śūraḥ śūreṇa saṃgamya saṃyugeṣv aparājitaḥc lakṣṇanena hataḥ śūraḥ putras te vibudhendrajita sa taṃ pratibhayaṃ śrutvā vadhaṃ putrasya dāruṇamc ghoram indrajitaḥ saṃkhye kaśmalaṃ prāviśan mahata upalabhya cirāt saṃjñāṃ rājā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥc putraśokārdito dīno vilalāpākulendriyaḥa hā rākṣasacamūmukhya mama vatsa mahārathac jitvendraṃ katham adya tvaṃ lakṣmaṇasya vaśaṃ gataḥa nanu tvam iṣubhiḥ kruddho bhindyāḥ kālāntakāv apic mandarasyāpi śṛṅgāṇi kiṃ punar lakṣmaṇaṃ raṇea adya vaivasvato rājā bhūyo bahumato mamac yenādya tvaṃ mahābāho saṃyuktaḥ kāladharmaṇāa eṣa panthāḥ suyodhānāṃ sarvāmaragaṇeṣv apic yaḥ kṛte hanyate bhartuḥ sa pumān svargam ṛcchatia adya devagaṇāḥ sarve lokapālās tatharṣayaḥc hatam indrajitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sukhaṃ svapsyanti nirbhayāḥa adya lokās trayaḥ kṛtsnāḥ pṛthivī ca sakānanāc ekenendrajitā hīnā śūṇyeva pratibhāti mea adya nairṛtakanyāyāṃ śroṣyāmy antaḥpure ravamc kareṇusaṃghasya yathā ninādaṃ girigahvarea yauvarājyaṃ ca laṅkāṃ ca rakṣāṃsi ca paraṃtapac mātaraṃ māṃ ca bhāryāṃ ca kva gato si vihāya naḥa mama nāma tvayā vīra gatasya yamasādanamc pretakāryāṇi kāryāṇi viparīte hi vartasea sa tvaṃ jīvati sugrīve rāghave ca salakṣmaṇec mama śalyam anuddhṛtya kva gato si vihāya naḥa evamādivilāpārtaṃ rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasādhipamc āviveśa mahān kopaḥ putravyasanasaṃbhavaḥa ghoraṃ prakṛtyā rūpaṃ tat tasya krodhāgnimūrchitamc babhūva rūpaṃ rudrasya kruddhasyeva durāsadama tasya kruddhasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatann asrabindavaḥc dīptābhyām iva dīpābhyāṃ sārciṣaḥ snehabindavaḥa dantān vidaśatas tasya śrūyate daśanasvanaḥc yantrasyāveṣṭyamānasya mahato dānavair ivaa kālāgnir iva saṃkruddho yāṃ yāṃ diśam avaikṣatac tasyāṃ tasyāṃ bhayatrastā rākṣasāḥ saṃnililyirea tam antakam iva kruddhaṃ carācaracikhādiṣumc vīkṣamāṇaṃ diśaḥ sarvā rākṣasā nopacakramuḥa tataḥ paramasaṃkruddho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥc abravīd rakṣasāṃ madhye saṃstambhayiṣur āhavea mayā varṣasahasrāṇi caritvā duścaraṃ tapaḥc teṣu teṣv avakāśeṣu svayambhūḥ paritoṣitaḥa tasyaiva tapaso vyuṣṭyā prasādāc ca svayambhuvaḥc nāsurebhyo na devebhyo bhayaṃ mama kadā canaa kavacaṃ brahmadattaṃ me yad ādityasamaprabhamc devāsuravimardeṣu na bhinnaṃ vajraśaktibhiḥa tena mām adya saṃyuktaṃ rathastham iha saṃyugec pratīyāt ko dya mām ājau sākṣād api puraṃdaraḥa yat tadābhiprasannena saśaraṃ kārmukaṃ mahatc devāsuravimardeṣu mama dattaṃ svayambhuvāa adya tūryaśatair bhīmaṃ dhanur utthāpyatāṃ mahatc rāmalakṣmaṇayor eva vadhāya paramāhavea sa putravadhasaṃtaptaḥ śūraḥ krodhavaśaṃ gataḥc samīkṣya rāvaṇo buddhyā sītāṃ hantuṃ vyavasyataa pratyavekṣya tu tāmrākṣaḥ sughoro ghoradarśanānc dīno dīnasvarān sarvāṃs tān uvāca niśācarāna māyayā mama vatsena vañcanārthaṃ vanaukasāmc kiṃ cid eva hataṃ tatra sīteyam iti darśitama tad idaṃ satyam evāhaṃ kariṣye priyam ātmanaḥc vaidehīṃ nāśayiṣyāmi kṣatrabandhum anuvratāme ity evam uktvā sacivān khaḍgam āśu parāmṛśata uddhṛtya guṇasaṃpannaṃ vimalāmbaravarcasaṃc niṣpapāta sa vegena sabhāyāḥ sacivair vṛtaḥa rāvaṇaḥ putraśokena bhṛśam ākulacetanaḥc saṃkruddhaḥ khaḍgam ādāya sahasā yatra maithilīa vrajantaṃ rākṣasaṃ prekṣya siṃhanādaṃ pracukruśuḥc ūcuś cānyonyam āśliṣya saṃkruddhaṃ prekṣya rākṣasāḥa adyainaṃ tāv ubhau dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau pravyathiṣyataḥc lokapālā hi catvāraḥ kruddhenānena nirjitāḥe bahavaḥ śatravaś cānye saṃyugeṣv abhipātitāḥa teṣāṃ saṃjalpamānānām aśokavanikāṃ gatāmc abhidudrāva vaidehīṃ rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥa vāryamāṇaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ suhṛdbhir hitabuddhibhiḥc abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ khe graho rohiṇīm ivaa maithilī rakṣyamāṇā tu rākṣasībhir aninditāc dadarśa rākṣasaṃ kruddhaṃ nistriṃśavaradhāriṇama taṃ niśāmya sanistriṃśaṃ vyathitā janakātmajāc nivāryamāṇaṃ bahuśaḥ suhṛdbhir anivartinama yathāyaṃ mām abhikruddhaḥ samabhidravati svayamc vadhiṣyati sanāthāṃ mām anāthām iva durmatiḥa bahuśaś codayām āsa bhartāraṃ mām anuvratāmc bhāryā bhava ramasyeti pratyākhyāto bhavan mayāa so yaṃ mām anupasthānād vyaktaṃ nairāśyam āgataḥc krodhamohasamāviṣṭo nihantuṃ māṃ samudyataḥa atha vā tau naravyāghrau bhrātarau rāmalakṣmaṇauc mannimittam anāryeṇa samare dya nipātitaue aho dhin mannimitto yaṃ vināśo rājaputrayoḥa hanūmato hi tadvākyaṃ na kṛtaṃ kṣudrayā mayāc yady ahaṃ tasya pṛṣṭhena tadāyāsam aninditāe nādyaivam anuśoceyaṃ bhartur aṅkagatā satīa manye tu hṛdayaṃ tasyāḥ kausalyāyāḥ phaliṣyatic ekaputrā yadā putraṃ vinaṣṭaṃ śroṣyate yudhia sā hi janma ca bālyaṃ ca yauvanaṃ ca mahātmanaḥc dharmakāryāṇi rūpaṃ ca rudatī saṃsramiṣyatia nirāśā nihate putre dattvā śrāddham acetanāc agnim ārokṣyate nūnam apo vāpi pravekṣyatia dhig astu kubjām asatīṃ mantharāṃ pāpaniścayāmc yannimittam idaṃ duḥkhaṃ kausalyā pratipatsyatea ity evaṃ maithilīṃ dṛṣṭvā vilapantīṃ tapasvinīmc rohiṇīm iva candreṇa vinā grahavaśaṃ gatāma supārśvo nāma medhāvī rāvaṇaṃ rākṣaseśvaramc nivāryamāṇaṃ sacivair idaṃ vacanam abravīta kathaṃ nāma daśagrīva sākṣād vaiśravaṇānujac hantum icchasi vaidehīṃ krodhād dharmam apāsya hia veda vidyāvrata snātaḥ svadharmanirataḥ sadāc striyāḥ kasmād vadhaṃ vīra manyase rākṣaseśvaraa maithilīṃ rūpasaṃpannāṃ pratyavekṣasva pārthivac tvam eva tu sahāsmābhī rāghave krodham utsṛjaa abhyutthānaṃ tvam adyaiva kṛṣṇapakṣacaturdaśīmc kṛtvā niryāhy amāvāsyāṃ vijayāya balair vṛtaḥa śūro dhīmān rathī khaḍgī rathapravaram āsthitaḥc hatvā dāśarathiṃ rāmaṃ bhavān prāpsyati maithilīma sa tad durātmā suhṛdā niveditaṃvacaḥ sudharmyaṃ pratigṛhya rāvaṇaḥc gṛhaṃ jagāmātha tataś ca vīryavānpunaḥ sabhāṃ ca prayayau suhṛdvṛtaḥa sa praviśya sabhāṃ rājā dīnaḥ paramaduḥkhitaḥc niṣasādāsane mukhye siṃhaḥ kruddha iva śvasana abravīc ca tadā sarvān balamukhyān mahābalaḥc rāvaṇaḥ prāñjalīn vākyaṃ putravyasanakarśitaḥa sarve bhavantaḥ sarveṇa hastyaśvena samāvṛtāḥc niryāntu rathasaṃghaiś ca pādātaiś copaśobhitāḥa ekaṃ rāmaṃ parikṣipya samare hantum arhathac prahṛṣṭā śaravarṣeṇa prāvṛṭkāla ivāmbudāḥa atha vāhaṃ śarair tīṣkṇair bhinnagātraṃ mahāraṇec bhavadbhiḥ śvo nihantāsmi rāmaṃ lokasya paśyataḥa ity evaṃ rākṣasendrasya vākyam ādāya rākṣasāḥc niryayus te rathaiḥ śīghraṃ nāgānīkaiś ca saṃvṛtāḥa sa saṃgrāmo mahābhīmaḥ sūryasyodayanaṃ pratic rakṣasāṃ vānarāṇāṃ ca tumulaḥ samapadyataa te gadābhir vicitrābhiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥc anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tadā vānararākṣasāḥa mātaṃgarathakūlasya vājimatsyā dhvajadrumāḥc śarīrasaṃghāṭavahāḥ prasasruḥ śoṇitāpagāḥa dhvajavarmarathān aśvān nānāpraharaṇāni cac āplutyāplutya samare vānarendrā babhañjirea keśān karṇalalāṭāṃś ca nāsikāś ca plavaṃgamāḥc rakṣasāṃ daśanais tīkṣṇair nakhaiś cāpi vyakartayana ekaikaṃ rākṣasaṃ saṃkhye śataṃ vānarapuṃgavāḥc abhyadhāvanta phalinaṃ vṛkṣaṃ śakunayo yathāa tathā gadābhir gurvībhiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥc nirjaghnur vānarān ghorān rākṣasāḥ parvatopamāḥa rākṣasair vadhyamānānāṃ vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūḥc śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yātā rāmaṃ daśarathātmajama tato rāmo mahātejā dhanur ādāya vīryavānc praviśya rākṣasaṃ sainyaṃ śaravarṣaṃ vavarṣa haa praviṣṭaṃ tu tadā rāmaṃ meghāḥ sūryam ivāmbarec nābhijagmur mahāghoraṃ nirdahantaṃ śarāgnināa kṛtāny eva sughorāṇi rāmeṇa rajanīcarāḥc raṇe rāmasya dadṛśuḥ karmāṇy asukarāṇi caa cālayantaṃ mahānīkaṃ vidhamantaṃ mahārathānc dadṛśus te na vai rāmaṃ vātaṃ vanagataṃ yathāa chinnaṃ bhinnaṃ śarair dagdhaṃ prabhagnaṃ śastrapīḍitamc balaṃ rāmeṇa dadṛśur na ramaṃ śīghrakāriṇama praharantaṃ śarīreṣu na te paśyanti rābhavamc indriyārtheṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ bhūtātmānam iva prajāḥa eṣa hanti gajānīkam eṣa hanti mahārathānc eṣa hanti śarais tīkṣṇaiḥ padātīn vājibhiḥ sahaa iti te rākṣasāḥ sarve rāmasya sadṛśān raṇec anyonyakupitā jaghnuḥ sādṛśyād rāghavasya tea na te dadṛśire rāmaṃ dahantam arivāhinīmc mohitāḥ paramāstreṇa gāndharveṇa mahātmanāa te tu rāma sahasrāṇi raṇe paśyanti rākṣasāḥc punaḥ paśyanti kākutstham ekam eva mahāhavea bhramantīṃ kāñcanīṃ koṭiṃ kārmukasya mahātmanaḥc alātacakrapratimāṃ dadṛśus te na rāghavama śarīranābhisattvārciḥ śarāraṃ nemikārmukamc jyāghoṣatalanirghoṣaṃ tejobuddhiguṇaprabhama divyāstraguṇaparyantaṃ nighnantaṃ yudhi rākṣasānc dadṛśū rāmacakraṃ tat kālacakram iva prajāḥa anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ rathānāṃ vātaraṃhasāmc aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvināma caturdaśasahasrāṇi sārohāṇāṃ ca vājināmc pūrṇe śatasahasre dve rākṣasānāṃ padātināma divasasyāṣṭame bhāge śarair agniśikhopamaiḥc hatāny ekena rāmeṇa rakṣasāṃ kāmarūpiṇāma te hatāśvā hatarathāḥ śrāntā vimathitadhvajāḥc abhipetuḥ purīṃ laṅkāṃ hataśeṣā niśācarāḥa hatair gajapadāty aśvais tad babhūva raṇājiramc ākrīḍabhūmī rudrasya kruddhasyeva pinākinaḥa tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥc sādhu sādhv iti rāmasya tat karma samapūjayana abravīc ca tadā rāmaḥ sugrīvaṃ pratyanantaramc etad astrabalaṃ divyaṃ mama vā tryambakasya vāa nihatya tāṃ rākṣasavāhinīṃ turāmas tadā śakrasamo mahātmāc astreṣu śastreṣu jitaklamaś casaṃstūyate devagaṇaiḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥa tāni nāgasahasrāṇi sārohāṇāṃ ca vājināmc rathānāṃ cāgnivarṇānāṃ sadhvajānāṃ sahasraśaḥa rākṣasānāṃ sahasrāṇi gadāparighayodhināmc kāñcanadhvajacitrāṇāṃ śūrāṇāṃ kāmarūpiṇāma nihatāni śarais tīkṣṇais taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥc rāvaṇena prayuktāni rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇāa dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca saṃbhrāntā hataśeṣā niśācarāḥc rākṣasyaś ca samāgamya dīnāś cintāpariplutāḥa vidhavā hataputrāś ca krośantyo hatabāndhavāḥc rākṣasyaḥ saha saṃgamya duḥkhārtāḥ paryadevayana kathaṃ śūrpaṇakhā vṛddhā karālā nirṇatodarīc āsasāda vane rāmaṃ kandarpam iva rūpiṇama sukumāraṃ mahāsattvaṃ sarvabhūtahite ratamc taṃ dṛṣṭvā lokavadhyā sā hīnarūpā prakāmitāa kathaṃ sarvaguṇair hīnā guṇavantaṃ mahaujasaṃc sumukhaṃ durmukhī rāmaṃ kāmayām āsa rākṣasīa janasyāsyālpabhāgyatvāt palinī śvetamūrdhajāc akāryam apahāsyaṃ ca sarvalokavigarhitama rākṣasānāṃ vināśāya dūṣaṇasya kharasya cac cakārāpratirūpā sā rāghavasya pradharṣaṇama tan nimittam idaṃ vairaṃ rāvaṇena kṛtaṃ mahatc vadhāya nītā sā sītā daśagrīveṇa rakṣasāa na ca sītāṃ daśagrīvaḥ prāpnoti janakātmajāmc baddhaṃ balavatā vairam akṣayaṃ rāghaveṇa haa vaidehīṃ prārthayānaṃ taṃ virādhaṃ prekṣya rākṣasaṃc hatam ekena rāmeṇa paryāptaṃ tannidarśanama caturdaśasahasrāṇi rakṣasāṃ bhīmakarmaṇāmc nihatāni janasthāne śarair agniśikhopamaiḥa kharaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye dūṣaṇas triśirās tathāc śarair ādityasaṃkāśaiḥ paryāptaṃ tannidarśanama hato yojanabāhuś ca kabandho rudhirāśanaḥc krodhārto vinadan so tha paryāptaṃ tannidarśanama jaghāna balinaṃ rāmaḥ sahasranayanātmajamc bālinaṃ meghasaṃkāśaṃ paryāptaṃ tannidarśanama ṛśyamūke vasañ śaile dīno bhagnamanorathaḥc sugrīvaḥ sthāpito rājye paryāptaṃ tannidarśanama dharmārthasahitaṃ vākyaṃ sarveṣāṃ rakṣasāṃ hitamc yuktaṃ vibhīṣaṇenoktaṃ mohāt tasya na rocatea vibhīṣaṇavacaḥ kuryād yadi sma dhanadānujaḥc śmaśānabhūtā duḥkhārtā neyaṃ laṅkā purī bhaveta kumbhakarṇaṃ hataṃ śrutvā rāghaveṇa mahābalamc priyaṃ cendrajitaṃ putraṃ rāvaṇo nāvabudhyatea mama putro mama bhrātā mama bhartā raṇe hataḥc ity evaṃ śrūyate śabdo rākṣasānāṃ kule kulea rathāś cāśvāś ca nāgāś ca hatāḥ śatasahasraśaḥc raṇe rāmeṇa śūreṇa rākṣasāś ca padātayaḥa rudro vā yadi vā viṣṇur mahendro vā śatakratuḥc hanti no rāmarūpeṇa yadi vā svayam antakaḥa hatapravīrā rāmeṇa nirāśā jīvite vayamc apaśyantyo bhayasyāntam anāthā vilapāmahea rāmahastād daśagrīvaḥ śūro dattavaro yudhic idaṃ bhayaṃ mahāghoram utpannaṃ nāvabudhyatea na devā na ca gandharvā na piśācā na rākasāḥc upasṛṣṭaṃ paritrātuṃ śaktā rāmeṇa saṃyugea utpātāś cāpi dṛśyante rāvaṇasya raṇe raṇec kathayiṣyanti rāmeṇa rāvaṇasya nibarhaṇama pitāmahena prītena devadānavarākṣasaiḥc rāvaṇasyābhayaṃ dattaṃ mānuṣebhyo na yācitama tad idaṃ mānuṣān manye prāptaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhayamc jīvitāntakaraṃ ghoraṃ rakṣasāṃ rāvaṇasya caa pīḍyamānās tu balinā varadānena rakṣasāc dīptais tapobhir vibudhāḥ pitāmaham apūjayana devatānāṃ hitārthāya mahātmā vai pitāmahaḥc uvāca devatāḥ sarvā idaṃ tuṣṭo mahad vacaḥa adya prabhṛti lokāṃs trīn sarve dānavarākṣasāḥc bhayena prāvṛtā nityaṃ vicariṣyanti śāśvatama daivatais tu samāgamya sarvaiś cendrapurogamaiḥc vṛṣadhvajas tripurahā mahādevaḥ prasāditaḥa prasannas tu mahādevo devān etad vaco bravītc utpatsyati hitārthaṃ vo nārī rakṣaḥkṣayāvahāa eṣā devaiḥ prayuktā tu kṣud yathā dānavān purāc bhakṣayiṣyati naḥ sītā rākṣasaghnī sarāvaṇāna rāvaṇasyāpanītena durvinītasya durmateḥc ayaṃ niṣṭānako ghoraḥ śokena samabhiplutaḥa taṃ na paśyāmahe loke yo naḥ śaraṇado bhavetc rāghaveṇopasṛṣṭānāṃ kāleneva yugakṣayea itīva sarvā rajanīcarastriyaḥparasparaṃ saṃparirabhya bāhubhiḥc viṣedur ārtātibhayābhipīḍitāvinedur uccaiś ca tadā sudāruṇama ārtānāṃ rākṣasīnāṃ tu laṅkāyāṃ vai kule kulec rāvaṇaḥ karuṇaṃ śabdaṃ śuśrāva pariveditama sa tu dīrghaṃ viniśvasya muhūrtaṃ dhyānam āsthitaḥc babhūva paramakruddho rāvaṇo bhīmadarśanaḥa saṃdaśya daśanair oṣṭhaṃ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥc rākṣasair api durdarśaḥ kālāgnir iva mūrchitaḥa uvāca ca samīpasthān rākṣasān rākṣaseśvaraḥc bhayāvyaktakathāṃs tatra nirdahann iva cakṣuṣāa mahodaraṃ mahāpārśvaṃ virūpākṣaṃ ca rākṣasaṃc śīghraṃ vadata sainyāni niryāteti mamājñayāa tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā rākṣasās te bhayārditāḥc codayām āsur avyagrān rākṣasāṃs tān nṛpājñayāa te tu sarve tathety uktvā rākṣasā ghoradarśanāḥc kṛtasvastyayanāḥ sarve rāvaṇābhimukhā yayuḥa pratipūjya yathānyāyaṃ rāvaṇaṃ te mahārathāḥc tasthuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve bhartur vijayakāṅkṣiṇaḥa athovāca prahasyaitān rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc mahodaramahāpārśvau virūpākṣaṃ ca rākṣasaṃa adya bāṇair dhanurmuktair yugāntādityasaṃnibhaiḥc rāghavaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ caiva neṣyāmi yamasādhanama kharasya kumbhakarṇasya prahastendrajitos tathāc kariṣyāmi pratīkāram adya śatruvadhād ahama naivāntarikṣaṃ na diśo na nadyo nāpi sāgaraḥc prakāśatvaṃ gamiṣyāmi madbāṇajaladāvṛtāḥa adya vānarayūthānāṃ tāni yūthāni bhāgaśaḥc dhanuḥsamudrād udbhūtair mathiṣyāmi śarormibhiḥa vyākośapadmacakrāṇi padmakesaravarcasāmc adya yūthataṭākāni gajavat pramathāmy ahama saśarair adya vadanaiḥ saṃkhye vānarayūthapāḥc maṇḍayiṣyanti vasudhāṃ sanālair iva paṅkalaiḥa adya yuddhapracaṇḍānāṃ harīṇāṃ drumayodhināmc muktenaikeṣuṇā yuddhe bhetsyāmi ca śataṃśatama hato bhartā hato bhrātā yāsāṃ ca tanayā hatāḥc vadhenādya ripos tāsāṃ karmomy asrapramārjanama adya madbāṇanirbhinnaiḥ prakīrṇair gatacetanaiḥc karomi vānarair yuddhe yatnāvekṣya talāṃ mahīma adya gomāyavo gṛdhrā ye ca māṃsāśino parec sarvāṃs tāṃs tarpayiṣyāmi śatrumāṃsaiḥ śarārditaiḥa kalpyatāṃ me rathaśīghraṃ kṣipram ānīyatāṃ dhanuḥc anuprayāntu māṃ yuddhe ye vaśiṣṭā niśācarāḥa tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā mahāpārśvo bravīd vacaḥc balādhyakṣān sthitāṃs tatra balaṃ saṃtvaryatām itia balādhyakṣās tu saṃrabdhā rākṣasāṃs tān gṛhād gṛhātc codayantaḥ pariyayur laṅkāṃ laghuparākramāḥa tato muhūrtān niṣpetū rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥc nardanto bhīmavadanā nānāpraharaṇair bhujaiḥa asibhiḥ paṭṭasaiḥ śūlair galābhir musalair halaiḥc śaktibhis tīkṣṇadhārābhir mahadbhiḥ kūṭamudgaraiḥa yaṣṭibhir vimalaiś cakrair niśitaiś ca paraśvadhaiḥc bhiṇḍipālaiḥ śataghnībhir anyaiś cāpi varāyudhaiḥa athānayan balādhyakṣāś catvāro rāvaṇājñayāc drutaṃ sūtasamāyuktaṃ yuktāṣṭaturagaṃ rathama āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasāc rāvaṇaḥ sattvagāmbhīryād dārayann iva medinīma rāvaṇenābhyanujñātau mahāpārśvamahodarauc virūpākṣaś ca durdharṣo rathān āruruhus tadāa te tu hṛṣṭā vinardanto bhindata iva medinīmc nādaṃ ghoraṃ vimuñcanto niryayur jayakāṅkṣiṇaḥa tato yuddhāya tejasvī rakṣogaṇabalair vṛtaḥc niryayāv udyatadhanuḥ kālāntakayamomapaḥa tataḥ prajavanāśvena rathena sa mahārathaḥc dvāreṇa niryayau tena yatra tau rāmalakṣmaṇaua tato naṣṭaprabhaḥ sūryo diśaś ca timirāvṛtāḥc dvijāś ca nedur ghorāś ca saṃcacāla ca medinīa vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devaś caskhaluś ca turaṃgamāḥc dhvajāgre nyapatad gṛdhro vineduś cāśivaṃ śivāḥa nayanaṃ cāsphurad vāmaṃ savyo bāhur akampatac vivarṇavadanaś cāsīt kiṃ cid abhraśyata svaraḥa tato niṣpatato yuddhe daśagrīvasya rakṣasaḥc raṇe nidhanaśaṃsīni rūpāṇy etāni jajñirea antarikṣāt papātolkā nirghātasamanisvanāc vinedur aśivaṃ gṛdhrā vāyasair anunāditāḥa etān acintayan ghorān utpātān samupasthitānc niryayau rāvaṇo mohād vadhārthī kālacoditaḥa teṣāṃ tu rathaghoṣeṇa rākṣasānāṃ mahātmanāmc vānarāṇām api camūr yuddhāyaivābhyavartataa teṣāṃ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ babhūva kapirakṣasāmc anyonyam āhvayānānāṃ kruddhānāṃ jayam icchatāma tataḥ kruddho daśagrīvaḥ śaraiḥ kāñcanabhūṣaṇaiḥc vānarāṇām anīkeṣu cakāra kadanaṃ mahata nikṛttaśirasaḥ ke cid rāvaṇena valīmukhāḥc nirucchvāsā hatāḥ ke cit ke cit pārśveṣu dāritāḥe ke cid vibhinnaśirasaḥ ke cic cakṣurvivarjitāḥa daśānanaḥ krodhavivṛttanetroyato yato bhyeti rathena saṃkhyec tatas tatas tasya śarapravegaṃsoḍhuṃ na śekur hariyūthapās tea tathā taiḥ kṛttagātrais tu daśagrīveṇa mārgaṇaiḥc babhūva vasudhā tatra prakīrṇā haribhir vṛtāa rāvaṇasyāprasahyaṃ taṃ śarasaṃpātam ekataḥc na śekuḥ sahituṃ dīptaṃ pataṃgā iva pāvakama te rditā niśitair bāṇaiḥ krośanto vipradudruvuḥc pāvakārciḥsamāviṣṭā dahyamānā yathā gajāḥa plavaṃgānām anīkāni mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥc sa yayau samare tasmin vidhaman rāvaṇaḥ śaraiḥa kadanaṃ tarasā kṛtvā rākṣasendro vanaukasāmc āsasāda tato yuddhe rāghavaṃ tvaritas tadāa sugrīvas tān kapīn dṛṣṭvā bhagnān vidravato raṇec gulme suṣeṇaṃ nikṣipya cakre yuddhe drutaṃ manaḥa ātmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ vīraṃ sa taṃ nikṣipya vānaramc sugrīvo bhimukhaḥ śatruṃ pratasthe pādapāyudhaḥa pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhataś cāsya sarve yūthādhipāḥ svayamc anujahrur mahāśailān vividhāṃś ca mahādrumāna sa nadan yudhi sugrīvaḥ svareṇa mahatā mahānc pātayan vividhāṃś cānyāñ jaghānottamarākṣasāna mamarda ca mahākāyo rākṣasān vānareśvaraḥc yugāntasamaye vāyuḥ pravṛddhān agamān ivaa rākṣasānām anīkeṣu śailavarṣaṃ vavarṣa hac aśvavarṣaṃ yathā meghaḥ pakṣisaṃgheṣu kānanea kapirājavimuktais taiḥ śailavarṣais tu rākṣasāḥc vikīrṇaśirasaḥ petur nikṛttā iva parvatāḥa atha saṃkṣīyamāṇeṣu rākṣaseṣu samantataḥc sugrīveṇa prabhagneṣu patatsu vinadatsu caa virūpākṣaḥ svakaṃ nāma dhanvī viśrāvya rākṣasaḥc rathād āplutya durdharṣo gajaskandham upāruhata sa taṃ dviradam āruhya virūpākṣo mahārathaḥc vinadan bhīmanirhrālaṃ vānarān abhyadhāvataa sugrīve sa śarān ghorān visasarja camūmukhec sthāpayām āsā codvignān rākṣasān saṃpraharṣayana so tividdhaḥ śitair bāṇaiḥ kapīndras tena rakṣasāc cukrodha ca mahākrodho vadhe cāsya mano dadhea tataḥ pādapam uddhṛtya śūraḥ saṃpradhane hariḥc abhipatya jaghānāsya pramukhe taṃ mahāgajama sa tu prahārābhihataḥ sugrīveṇa mahāgajaḥc apāsarpad dhanurmātraṃ niṣasāda nanāda caa gajāt tu mathitāt tūrṇam apakramya sa vīryavānc rākṣaso bhimukhaḥ śatruṃ pratyudgamya tataḥ kapima ārṣabhaṃ carmakhaḍgaṃ ca pragṛhya laghuvikramaḥc bhartsayann iva sugrīvam āsasāda vyavasthitama sa hi tasyābhisaṃkruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ śilāmc virūpākṣāya cikṣepa sugrīvo jaladopamāma sa tāṃ śilām āpatantīṃ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasapuṃgavaḥc apakramya suvikrāntaḥ khaḍgena prāharat tadāa tena khaḍgena saṃkruddhaḥ sugrīvasya camūmukhec kavacaṃ pātayām āsa sa khaḍgābhihato patata sa samutthāya patitaḥ kapis tasya vyasarjayatc talaprahāram aśaneḥ samānaṃ bhīmanisvanama talaprahāraṃ tad rakṣaḥ sugrīveṇa samudyatamc naipuṇyān mocayitvainaṃ muṣṭinorasy atāḍayata tatas tu saṃkruddhataraḥ sugrīvo vānareśvaraḥc mokṣitaṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā prahāraṃ tena rakṣasāa sa dadarśāntaraṃ tasya virūpākṣasya vānaraḥc tato nyapātayat krodhāc chaṅkhadeśe mahātalama mahendrāśanikalpena talenābhihataḥ kṣitauc papāta rudhiraklinnaḥ śoṇitaṃ sa samudvamana vivṛttanayanaṃ krodhāt saphena rudhirāplutamc dadṛśus te virūpākṣaṃ virūpākṣataraṃ kṛtama sphurantaṃ parivarjantaṃ pārśvena rudhirokṣitamc karuṇaṃ ca vinardāntaṃ dadṛśuḥ kapayo ripuma tathā tu tau saṃyati saṃprayuktautarasvinau vānararākṣasānāmc balārṇavau sasvanatuḥ sabhīmaṃmahārṇavau dvāv iva bhinnavelaua vināśitaṃ prekṣya virūpanetraṃmahābalaṃ taṃ haripārthivenac balaṃ samastaṃ kapirākṣasānāmunmattagaṅgāpratimaṃ babhūvaa hanyamāne bale tūrṇam anyonyaṃ te mahāmṛdhec sarasīva mahāgharme sūpakṣīṇe babhūvatuḥa svabalasya vighātena virūpākṣavadhena cac babhūva dviguṇaṃ kruddho rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥa prakṣīṇaṃ tu balaṃ dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānaṃ valīmukhaiḥc babhūvāsya vyathā yuddhe prekṣya daivaviparyayama uvāca ca samīpasthaṃ mahodaram ariṃdamamc asmin kāle mahābāho jayāśā tvayi me sthitāa jahi śatrucamūṃ vīra darśayādya parākramamc bhartṛpiṇḍasya kālo yaṃ nirveṣṭuṃ sādhu yudhyatāma evam uktas tathety uktvā rākṣasendraṃ mahodaraḥc praviveśārisenāṃ sa pataṃga iva pāvakama tataḥ sa kadanaṃ cakre vānarāṇāṃ mahābalaḥc bhartṛvākyena tejasvī svena vīryeṇa coditaḥa prabhagnāṃ samare dṛṣṭvā vānarāṇāṃ mahācamūmc abhidudrāva sugrīvo mahodaram anantarama pragṛhya vipulāṃ ghorāṃ mahīdhara samāṃ śilāmc cikṣepa ca mahātejās tad vadhāya harīśvaraḥa tām āpatantīṃ sahasā śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā mahodaraḥc asaṃbhrāntas tato bāṇair nirbibheda durāsadāma rakṣasā tena bāṇaughair nikṛttā sā sahasradhāc nipapāta śilābhūmau gṛdhracakram ivākulama tāṃ tu bhinnāṃ śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā sugrīvaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc sālam utpāṭya cikṣepa rakṣase raṇamūrdhanie śaraiś ca vidadārainaṃ śūraḥ parapuraṃjayaḥa sa dadarśa tataḥ kruddhaḥ parighaṃ patitaṃ bhuvic āvidhya tu sa taṃ dīptaṃ parighaṃ tasya darśayane parighāgreṇa vegena jaghānāsya hayottamāna tasmād dhatahayād vīraḥ so vaplutya mahārathātc gadāṃ jagrāha saṃkruddho rākṣaso tha mahodaraḥa gadāparighahastau tau yudhi vīrau samīyatuḥc nardantau govṛṣaprakhyau ghanāv iva savidyutaua ājaghāna gadāṃ tasya parigheṇa harīśvaraḥc papāta sa gadodbhinnaḥ parighas tasya bhūtalea tato jagrāha tejasvī sugrīvo vasudhātalātc āyasaṃ musalaṃ ghoraṃ sarvato hemabhūṣitama taṃ samudyamya cikṣepa so py anyāṃ vyākṣipad gadāmc bhinnāv anyonyam āsādya petatur dharaṇītalea tato bhagnapraharaṇau muṣṭibhyāṃ tau samīyatuḥc tejo balasamāviṣṭau dīptāv iva hutāśanaua jaghnatus tau tadānyonyaṃ nedatuś ca punaḥ punaḥc talaiś cānyonyam āhatya petatur dharaṇītalea utpetatus tatas tūrṇaṃ jaghnatuś ca parasparamc bhujaiś cikṣepatur vīrāv anyonyam aparājitaua ājahāra tadā khagḍam adūraparivartinamc rākṣasaś carmaṇā sārdhaṃ mahāvego mahodaraḥa tathaiva ca mahākhaḍgaṃ carmaṇā patitaṃ sahac jagrāha vānaraśreṣṭhaḥ sugrīvo vegavattaraḥa tau tu roṣaparītāṅgau nardantāv abhyadhāvatāmc udyatāsī raṇe hṛṣṭau yudhi śastraviśāradaua dakṣiṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ cobhau tau tūrṇaṃ saṃparīyatuḥc anyonyam abhisaṃkruddhau jaye praṇihitāv ubhaua sa tu śūro mahāvego vīryaślāghī mahodaraḥc mahācarmaṇi taṃ khaḍgaṃ pātayām āsa durmatiḥa lagnam utkarṣataḥ khaḍgaṃ khaḍgena kapikuñjaraḥc jahāra saśiras trāṇaṃ kuṇḍalopahitaṃ śiraḥa nikṛttaśirasas tasya patitasya mahītalec tad balaṃ rākṣasendrasya dṛṣṭvā tatra na tiṣṭhatia hatvā taṃ vānaraiḥ sārdhaṃ nanāda mudito hariḥc cukrodha ca daśagrīvo babhau hṛṣṭaś ca rāghavaḥa mahodare tu nihate mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥc aṅgadasya camūṃ bhīmāṃ kṣobhayām āsa sāyakaiḥa sa vānarāṇāṃ mukhyānām uttamāṅgāni sarvaśaḥc pātayām āsa kāyebhyaḥ phalaṃ vṛntād ivānilaḥa keṣāṃ cid iṣubhir bāhūn skandhāṃś cicheda rākṣasaḥc vānarāṇāṃ susaṃkruddhaḥ pārśvaṃ keṣāṃ vyadārayata te rditā bāṇavarṣeṇa mahāpārśvena vānarāḥc viṣādavimukhāḥ sarve babhūvur gatacetasaḥa nirīkṣya balam udvignam aṅgado rākṣasārditamc vegaṃ cakre mahābāhuḥ samudra iva parvaṇia āyasaṃ parighaṃ gṛhya sūryaraśmisamaprabhamc samare vānaraśreṣṭho mahāpārśve nyapātayata sa tu tena prahāreṇa mahāpārśvo vicetanaḥc sasūtaḥ syandanāt tasmād visaṃjñaḥ prāpatad bhuvia sarkṣarājas tu tejasvī nīlāñjanacayopamaḥc niṣpatya sumahāvīryaḥ svād yūthān meghasaṃnibhāta pragṛhya giriśṛṅgābhāṃ kruddhaḥ sa vipulāṃ śilāmc aśvāñ jaghāna tarasā syandanaṃ ca babhañja tama muhūrtāl labdhasaṃjñas tu mahāpārśvo mahābalaḥc aṅgadaṃ bahubhir bāṇair bhūyas taṃ pratyavidhyataa jāmbavantaṃ tribhir bāṇair ājaghāna stanāntarec ṛkṣarājaṃ gavākṣaṃ ca jaghāna bahubhiḥ śaraiḥa gavākṣaṃ jāmbavantaṃ ca sa dṛṣṭvā śarapīḍitauc jagrāha parighaṃ ghoram aṅgadaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥa tasyāṅgadaḥ prakupito rākṣasasya tam āyasaṃc dūrasthitasya parighaṃ raviraśmisamaprabhama dvābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ saṃgṛhya bhrāmayitvā ca vegavānc mahāpārśvāya cikṣepa vadhārthaṃ vālinaḥ sutaḥa sa tu kṣipto balavatā parighas tasya rakṣasaḥc dhanuś ca saśaraṃ hastāc chirastraṃ cāpy apātayata taṃ samāsādya vegena vāliputraḥ pratāpavānc talenābhyahanat kruddhaḥ karṇamūle sakuṇḍalea sa tu kruddho mahāvego mahāpārśvo mahādyutiḥc kareṇaikena jagrāha sumahāntaṃ paraśvadhama taṃ tailadhautaṃ vimalaṃ śailasāramayaṃ dṛḍhamc rākṣasaḥ paramakruddho vāliputre nyapātayata tena vāmāṃsaphalake bhṛśaṃ pratyavapātitamc aṅgado mokṣayām āsa saroṣaḥ sa paraśvadhama sa vīro vajrasaṃkāśam aṅgado muṣṭim ātmanaḥc saṃvartayan susaṃkruddhaḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥa rākṣasasya stanābhyāśe marmajño hṛdayaṃ pratic indrāśanisamasparśaṃ sa muṣṭiṃ vinyapātayata tena tasya nipātena rākṣasasya mahāmṛdhec paphāla hṛdayaṃ cāśu sa papāta hato bhuvia tasmin nipatite bhūmau tat sainyaṃ saṃpracukṣubhec abhavac ca mahān krodhaḥ samare rāvaṇasya tua mahodaramahāpārśvau hatau dṛṣṭvā tu rākṣasauc tasmiṃś ca nihate vīre virūpākṣe mahābalea āviveśa mahān krodho rāvaṇaṃ tu mahāmṛdhec sūtaṃ saṃcodayām āsa vākyaṃ cedam uvāca haa nihatānām amātyānāṃ ruddhasya nagarasya cac duḥkham eṣo paneṣyāmi hatvā tau rāmalakṣmaṇaua rāmavṛkṣaṃ raṇe hanmi sītāpuṣpaphalapradamc praśākhā yasya sugrīvo jāmbavān kumudo nalaḥa sa diśo daśa ghoṣeṇa rathasyātiratho mahānc nādayan prayayau tūrṇaṃ rāghavaṃ cābhyavartataa pūritā tena śabdena sanadīgirikānanāc saṃcacāla mahī sarvā savarāhamṛgadvipāa tāmasaṃ sumahāghoraṃ cakārāstraṃ sudāruṇamc nirdadāha kapīn sarvāṃs te prapetuḥ samantataḥa tāny anīkāny anekāni rāvaṇasya śarottamaiḥc dṛṣṭvā bhagnāni śataśo rāghavaḥ paryavasthitaḥa sa dadarśa tato rāmaṃ tiṣṭhantam aparājitamc lakṣmaṇena saha bhrātrā viṣṇunā vāsavaṃ yathāa ālikhantam ivākāśam avaṣṭabhya mahad dhanuḥc padmapatraviśālākṣaṃ dīrghabāhum ariṃdamama vānarāṃś ca raṇe bhagnān āpatantaṃ ca rāvaṇamc samīkṣya rāghavo hṛṣṭo madhye jagrāha kārmukama visphārayitum ārebhe tataḥ sa dhanur uttamamc mahāvegaṃ mahānādaṃ nirbhindann iva medinīma tayoḥ śarapathaṃ prāpya rāvaṇo rājaputrayoḥc sa babhūva yathā rāhuḥ samīpe śaśisūryayoḥa rāvaṇasya ca bāṇaughai rāmavispharitena cac śabdena rākṣasās tena petuś ca śataśas tadāa tam icchan prathamaṃ yoddhuṃ lakṣmaṇo niśitaiḥ śaraiḥc mumoca dhanur āyamya śarān agniśikhopamāna tān muktamātrān ākāśe lakṣmaṇena dhanuṣmatāc bāṇān bāṇair mahātejā rāvaṇaḥ pratyavārayata ekam ekena bāṇena tribhis trīn daśabhir daśac lakṣmaṇasya praciccheda darśayan pāṇilāghavama abhyatikramya saumitriṃ rāvaṇaḥ samitiṃjayaḥc āsasāda tato rāmaṃ sthitaṃ śailam ivācalama sa saṃkhye rāmam āsādya krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥc vyasṛjac charavarṇāni rāvaṇo rāghavoparia śaradhārās tato rāmo rāvaṇasya dhanuścyutāḥc dṛṣṭvaivāpatitāḥ śīghraṃ bhallāñ jagrāha satvarama tāñ śaraughāṃs tato bhallais tīkṣṇaiś ciccheda rāghavaḥc dīpyamānān mahāvegān kruddhān āśīviṣān ivaa rāghavo rāvaṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ rāvaṇo rāghavaṃ tathāc anyonyaṃ vividhais tīkṣṇaiḥ śarair abhivavarṣatuḥa ceratuś ca ciraṃ citraṃ maṇḍalaṃ savyadakṣiṇamc bāṇavegān samudīkṣya samareṣv aparājitaua tayor bhūtāni vitreṣur yugapat saṃprayudhyatoḥc raudrayoḥ sāyakamucor yamāntakanikāśayoḥa saṃtataṃ vividhair bāṇair babhūva gaganaṃ tadāc ghanair ivātapāpāye vidyunmālāsamākulaiḥa gavākṣitam ivākāśaṃ babhūva śūravṛṣṭibhiḥc mahāvegaiḥ sutīkṣṇāgrair gṛdhrapatraiḥ suvājitaiḥa śarāndhakāraṃ tau bhīmaṃ cakratuḥ paramaṃ tadāc gate staṃ tapane cāpi mahāmeghāv ivotthitaua babhūva tumulaṃ yuddham anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇoḥc anāsādyam acintyaṃ ca vṛtravāsavayor ivaa ubhau hi parameṣvāsāv ubhau śastraviśāradauc ubhau cāstravidāṃ mukhyāv ubhau yuddhe viceratuḥa ubhau hi yena vrajatas tena tena śarormayaḥc ūrmayo vāyunā viddhā jagmuḥ sāgarayor ivaa tataḥ saṃsaktahastas tu rāvaṇo lokarāvaṇaḥc nārācamālāṃ rāmasya lalāṭe pratyamuñcataa raudracāpaprayuktāṃ tāṃ nīlotpaladalaprabhāmc śirasā dhārayan rāmo na vyathāṃ pratyapadyataa atha mantrān api japan raudram astram udīrayanc śarān bhūyaḥ samādāya rāmaḥ krodhasamanvitaḥa mumoca ca mahātejāś cāpam āyamya vīryavānc tāñ śarān rākṣasendrāya cikṣepācchinnasāyakaḥa te mahāmeghasaṃkāśe kavace patitāḥ śarāḥc avadhye rākṣasendrasya na vyathāṃ janayaṃs tadāa punar evātha taṃ rāmo rathasthaṃ rākṣasādhipamc lalāṭe paramāstreṇa sarvāstrakuśalo bhinata te bhittvā bāṇarūpāṇi pañcaśīrṣā ivoragāḥc śvasanto viviśur bhūmiṃ rāvaṇapratikūlatāḥa nihatya rāghavasyāstraṃ rāvaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥc āsuraṃ sumahāghoram anyad astraṃ samādadea siṃhavyāghramukhāṃś cānyān kaṅkakāka mukhān apic gṛdhraśyenamukhāṃś cāpi sṛgālavadanāṃs tathāa īhāmṛgamuhāṃś cānyān vyāditāsyān bhayāvahānc pañcāsyāṃl lelihānāṃś ca sasarja niśitāñ śarāna śarān kharamukhāṃś cānyān varāhamukhasaṃsthitānc śvānakukkuṭavaktrāṃś ca makarāśīviṣānanāna etāṃś cānyāṃś ca māyābhiḥ sasarja niśitāñ śarānc rāmaṃ prati mahātejāḥ kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasana āsureṇa samāviṣṭaḥ so streṇa raghunandanaḥc sasarjāstraṃ mahotsāhaḥ pāvakaṃ pāvakopamaḥa agnidīptamukhān bāṇāṃs tathā sūryamukhān apic candrārdhacandravaktrāṃś ca dhūmaketumukhān apia grahanakṣatravarṇāṃś ca maholkā mukhasaṃsthitānc vidyujjihvopamāṃś cānyān sasarja niśitāñ śarāna te rāvaṇaśarā ghorā rāghavāstrasamāhatāḥc vilayaṃ jagmur ākāśe jagmuś caiva sahasraśaḥa tad astraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇāc hṛṣṭā nedus tataḥ sarve kapayaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥa tasmin pratihate stre tu rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥc krodhaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ cakre krodhāc cāstram anantarama mayena vihitaṃ raudram anyad astraṃ mahādyutiḥc utsraṣṭuṃ rāvaṇo ghoraṃ rāghavāya pracakramea tataḥ śūlāni niścerur gadāś ca musalāni cac kārmukād dīpyamānāni vajrasārāṇi sarvaśaḥa kūṭamudgarapāśāś ca dīptāś cāśanayas tathāc niṣpetur vividhās tīkṣṇā vātā iva yugakṣayea tad astraṃ rāghavaḥ śrīmān uttamāstravidāṃ varaḥc jaghāna paramāstreṇa gandharveṇa mahādyutiḥa tasmin pratihate stre tu rāghaveṇa mahātmanāc rāvaṇaḥ krodhatāmrākṣaḥ sauram astram udīrayata tataś cakrāṇi niṣpetur bhāsvarāṇi mahānti cac kārmukād bhīmavegasya daśagrīvasya dhīmataḥa tair āsīd gaganaṃ dīptaṃ saṃpatadbhir itas tataḥc patadbhiś ca diśo dīptaiś candrasūryagrahair ivaa tāni ciccheda bāṇaughaiś cakrāṇi tu sa rāghavaḥc āyudhāni vicitrāṇi rāvaṇasya camūmukhea tad astraṃ tu hataṃ dṛṣṭvā rāvaṇo rākṣasādhipaḥc vivyādha daśabhir bāṇai rāmaṃ sarveṣu marmasua sa viddho daśabhir bāṇair mahākārmukaniḥsṛtaiḥc rāvaṇena mahātejā na prākampata rāghavaḥa tato vivyādha gātreṣu sarveṣu samitiṃjayaḥc rāghavas tu susaṃkruddho rāvaṇaṃ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥa etasminn antare kruddho rāghavasyānujo balīc lakṣmaṇaḥ sāyakān sapta jagrāha paravīrahāa taiḥ sāyakair mahāvegai rāvaṇasya mahādyutiḥc dhvajaṃ manuṣyaśīrṣaṃ tu tasya ciccheda naikadhāa sāratheś cāpi bāṇena śiro jvalitakuṇḍalamc jahāra lakṣmaṇaḥ śrīmān nairṛtasya mahābalaḥa tasya bāṇaiś ca ciccheda dhanur gajakaropamamc lakṣmaṇo rākṣasendrasya pañcabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥa nīlameghanibhāṃś cāsya sadaśvān parvatopamānc jaghānāplutya gadayā rāvaṇasya vibhīṣaṇaḥa hatāśvād vegavān vegād avaplutya mahārathātc krodham āhārayat tīvraṃ bhrātaraṃ prati rāvaṇaḥa tataḥ śaktiṃ mahāśaktir dīptāṃ dīptāśanīm ivac vibhīṣaṇāya cikṣepa rākṣasendraḥ pratāpavāna aprāptām eva tāṃ bāṇais tribhiś ciccheda lakṣmaṇaḥc athodatiṣṭhat saṃnādo vānarāṇāṃ tadā raṇea sa papāta tridhā chinnā śaktiḥ kāñcanamālinīc savisphuliṅgā jvalitā maholkeva divaś cyutāa tataḥ saṃbhāvitatarāṃ kālenāpi durāsadāmc jagrāha vipulāṃ śaktiṃ dīpyamānāṃ svatejasāa sā veginā balavatā rāvaṇena durātmanāc jajvāla sumahāghorā śakrāśanisamaprabhāa etasminn antare vīro lakṣmaṇas taṃ vibhīṣaṇamc prāṇasaṃśayam āpannaṃ tūrṇam evābhyapadyataa taṃ vimokṣayituṃ vīraś cāpam āyamya lakṣmaṇaḥc rāvaṇaṃ śaktihastaṃ taṃ śaravarṣair avākirata kīryamāṇaḥ śaraugheṇa visṛṣṭtena mahātmanāc na prahartuṃ manaś cakre vimukhīkṛtavikramaḥa mokṣitaṃ bhrātaraṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇena sa rāvaṇaḥc lakṣmaṇābhimukhas tiṣṭhann idaṃ vacanam abravīta mokṣitas te balaślāghin yasmād evaṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥc vimucya rākṣasaṃ śaktis tvayīyaṃ vinipātyatea eṣā te hṛdayaṃ bhittvā śaktir lohitalakṣaṇāc madbāhuparighotsṛṣṭā prāṇān ādāya yāsyatia ity evam uktvā tāṃ śaktim aṣṭaghaṇṭāṃ mahāsvanāmc mayena māyāvihitām amoghāṃ
